### NORMALIZED CONTENT

This chapter contains a detailed list of all the contents of the installation bundles for the version 19.0 SP4 release, along with respective file locations.

This chapter does not contain links to software downloads. For software download instructions, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].

## PAGE 00004: 3DS Media list for 2021x Refresh2 HF5 release

- page_id: `136726120`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726120/3DS+Media+list+for+2021x+Refresh2+HF5+release

- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Downloading installation files
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

This chapter contains a detailed list of all the contents of the installation bundles for the version 2021x Refresh2 HF5 release, along with respective file locations.

This chapter does not contain links to software downloads.

volumes

| CATIA Magic portfolio | No Magic portfolio | CATIA Magic Academic portfolio |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  |  |  |

##### How to download your software

To access your download page, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].

Navigate to CATIA, No Magic, release **NoMagic 2021x,** select level **NoMagic 2021x****Refresh2,** and select the "Fixes for this Level" **No Magic 2021x Refresh2 HF5**.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

This chapter contains a detailed list of all the contents of the installation bundles for the version 2022x Refresh1 release, along with respective file locations.

This chapter does not contain links to software downloads. For software download instructions, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].

| --- | --- | --- |
|  |  |  |

##### CATIA Magic portfolio media volume content

All plugins provided by us, both commercial and no-cost, are pre-bundled together with the installation files and are available to install from the **Resource/Plugin Manager**. See the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing plugins' space=''] page.

## PAGE 00007: 3DS Media list for 2022x Refresh2 release

- page_id: `136726117`

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

This chapter contains a detailed list of all the contents of the installation bundles for the version 2022x Refresh2 release, along with respective file locations.

This chapter does not contain links to software downloads. For software download instructions, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].

volumes

| --- | --- | --- |
|  |  |  |

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

This chapter contains a detailed list of all the contents of the installation bundles for the version 2022x release, along with respective file locations.

This chapter does not contain links to software downloads. For software download instructions, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

This chapter contains a detailed list of all the contents of the installation bundles for the version 2024x Hot Fix 3 release, along with respective file locations.

This chapter does not contain links to software downloads. For software download instructions, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].

volumes

| CATIA Magic portfolio | No Magic portfolio | CATIA Magic Academic portfolio |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  |  |  |

##### CATIA Magic portfolio media volume content

All plugins provided by us, both commercial and no-cost, are pre-bundled together with the installation files and are available to install from the **Resource/Plugin Manager**. See the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing plugins' space=''] page.

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

This chapter contains a detailed list of all the contents of the installation bundles for the version 2024x release, along with respective file locations.

This chapter does not contain links to software downloads. For software download instructions, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726266 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00012: Adding a license to the FlexNet server

- page_id: `136726266`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726266/Adding+a+license+to+the+FlexNet+server
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:21.475+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

451351663

451351675

451351665

INLINE

##### Prerequisites

- The FlexNet license server is installed.
- You have the license key.

##### Procedure

1. Start the FlexNet license server.
2. Import the license key to the FlexNet license server.

To import the license key to the FlexNet license server:

1. Connect to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface. Use the default address ([http://localhost:8090](http://localhost:8090/)) or your server name (http://<server name>:8090).
2. Click Administration at the top-right corner of the webpage. When prompted to sign in, enter the default administrator's credentials (admin/admin).
3. In the FlexNet License Administrator's webpage, click Vendor Daemon Configuration on the left.
4. Click Import License and select the received license key file.
5. Click the **Import License** button. If you want to re-import the license key file, select the **Overwrite License File on License Server** check box. [IMAGE alt='' src='']

451351662

**Related pages**

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Host ID or Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed' space='IL2024x']

## PAGE 00013: Adding the license key

- page_id: `136726221`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726221/Adding+the+license+key
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:19.538+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Modeling tools and plugins licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

393675900

393675903

393675902

INLINE

To add the license key

1. In the <modeling tool> License Manager dialog, click the Select License Key Files button.
2. In the Select License Key File dialog, select the license key file.
3. Click Open .

To check the license information at a later time, select **Help** > **About** and click the **Licensing** tab in the open dialog.

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726188 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00014: Basic concepts

- page_id: `136726188`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726188/Basic+concepts
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:17.636+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

390931863

390931867

390931865

| Concept | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Borrowing | Using a floating license in the offline mode.If a license is used on a machine that is intermittently connected to the license server, the license can be borrowed from the server and used as an offline floating license. A license can be borrowed from a license server for the selected period of time (default 24 hours).The maximum license borrowing period is 2 months. If you would like to limit the maximum borrowing period, please contact your sales representative. |
| Configuration files | The files where your defined settings and environment options are stored.When upgrading your software, you can choose one of the following:If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool or server version, select the location and click Import.If you are installing the software for the first time and/or do not want to use earlier environment options, click Use Default. |
| License key | A license for the dedicated Target ID received after purchase. |
| Floating license | The floating license allows you to install and use the same license on multiple machines. Both DSLS and FlexNet license server are used to manage floating licenses. |
| HostID/TargetIDTarget ID / Host ID / Computer ID | A combination of numbers and letters (also known as the MAC Address or Physical Address), which identifies the network card of a machine. It is used to tie the license to a particular machine. The Host ID is for the FlexNet license server, and the Computer ID is for DSLS. |
| License type | Seat (Nodelock). The license of a modeling tool dedicated to one working place.Floating (Shareable). Allows you to install and use the same license of a modeling tool on multiple machines.Managed. Allows you to obtain license keys from a highly available license server managed by Dassault Systemes (SaaS), which is not installed on your premises.Please note that the license type of a modeling tool and the plugins used with the tool must be the same. |
| vendor daemonVendor daemon | A program developed by CATIA / No Magic to implement the FlexNet license server. The vendor daemon tracks how many licenses are checked out and who has the licenses. |

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726265 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00015: Checking if the FlexNet server is running

- page_id: `136726265`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726265/Checking+if+the+FlexNet+server+is+running
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:21.357+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

INLINE

There are three ways to check if the FlexNet server is running:

1. Log on to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface. The default address is http://localhost:8090 or use your server name ( http://<server name>:8090 ). If connection is established, the FlexNet server is running.
2. Check the lmadmin task status in: If the status is Running , the FlexNet server is running.
  - Task Manager on Windows
  - Activity Monitor on OS X
  - System Monitor on Linux
3. Open the *lmadmin.log* file which can be found in *<lmadmin installation directory>\logs*. Lines in the following example identify that *lmadmin* is successfully started and the FlexNet server is running: 2015-12-09 20:28:31,781 root.LicenseEngine started without redundancy. 2015-12-09 20:28:31,958 root.Vendor (cameo) started. 2015-12-09 20:28:31,778 root Version: 11.13.1.0 build 166859 (2015.06.16-10.40.53)

If the FlexNet server is not running, open the *lmadmin.log* file, found in *<lmadmin installation directory>\logs.* The installation error codes are listed there. Use the error codes to try to find a solution in the FlexNet server License Administration Guide:

- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.18.2.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf']

If you still can't identify the server starting problem, please contact our [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Support_obsolete' space='NMDOC'].

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="excerpt" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="6fa9bea3-d8a8-4dad-9f9c-d6737d4091fa"><ac:parameter ac:name="atlassian-macro-output-type">INLINE</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p><span style="color: rgb(51,51,51);"><ac:inline-comment-marker ac:ref="1a83de3b-8a96-457b-b35d-2faee43746db">There are three ways to check if the FlexNet server is running</ac:inline-comment-marker>:</span></p><ol><li>Log on  to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface. The default address is <a href="http://localhost:8090/">http://localhost:8090</a> or use your server name (<em>http://&lt;server name&gt;:8090</em>). If connection is established, the FlexNet server is running. </li><li>Check the <em>lmadmin</em> task status in:<ul><li>Task Manager on Windows</li><li>Activity Monitor on OS X</li><li>System Monitor on Linux</li></ul>If the status is <em>Running</em>, the FlexNet server is running.</li><li><p>Open the <em>lmadmin.log</em> file which can be found in <em>&lt;lmadmin installation directory&gt;\logs</em>. Lines in the following example identify that <em>lmadmin</em> is successfully started and the FlexNet server is running:</p><pre>2015-12-09 20:28:31,781 root.LicenseEngine started without redundancy.</pre><pre>2015-12-09 20:28:31,958 root.Vendor (cameo) started.</pre><pre>2015-12-09 20:28:31,778 root Version: 11.13.1.0 build 166859 (2015.06.16-10.40.53)</pre><p><br /></p></li></ol><p>If the FlexNet server is not running, open the <em>lmadmin.log</em> file, found in <em>&lt;lmadmin installation directory&gt;\logs.</em> The installation error codes are listed there. Use the error codes to try to find a solution in the FlexNet server License Administration Guide:</p><ul><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2022 R1 (11.19.0)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11.18.2.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2021 R3 (11.18.2)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2020 R2 (11.17.0)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2019 R2 (11.16.4)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2014 R1 (11.12.1)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li></ul><p>If you still can't identify the server starting problem, please contact our <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Support_obsolete" ri:space-key="NMDOC" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[support team]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p><p><br /></p>
````

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726282 space=IL2024x version=2 -->
## PAGE 00016: Creating modeling tools bundle

- page_id: `136726282`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726282/Creating+modeling+tools+bundle
- version_number: 2
- version_date: `2025-10-21T09:47:38.322+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Modeling tools bundle
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

##### Creating a modeling tools bundle (instructions for an Administrator)

To create a modeling tools bundle

1. Install a modeling tool:
  1. Double click <modeling_tool_name>_<version_number>win.exe or <modeling_tool_name>*<version_* number>win64.exe .
  2. In the opened dialog, select a language and click OK . The modeling tool installation wizard opens.
  3. In the first and second steps, click Next .
  4. Select the memory allocation mode and click Next .
  5. Choose the modeling tool installation folder and click Next .
  6. If needed, choose to create modeling tool icons and click Install .
  7. Do NOT check the box to launch the modeling tool, then click Done . The modeling tool is installed.
2. Change the modeling tool's configuration files location so that the configuration files would be located in the modeling tool's installation folder:
  1. Open the <modeling_tool_name>.properties file in the <modeling tool installation>/bin folder (e.g., C:/Program Files/<modeling_tool_name>/bin ).
  2. Once you open the properties file, locate the line that starts with JAVA_ARGS=
    1. Find –DLOCALCONFIG\= true and change the option value to false ; i.e., – DLOCALCONFIG\=false
    2. **Add the following parameter: -*DWINCONFIG\=false*(Do not change any of the parameters in the *JAVA_ARGS* line during this step). Example of the 2 parameters after the changes are complete: 
*JAVA_ARGS=-Xmx12000M******-DLOCALCONFIG\=false************-DWINCONFIG\=false**********…*
  3. Save the <modeling_tool_name> . properties file. The configuration files are saved in the modeling tool's installation folder.
3. Start the modeling tool and apply a license. If the person building the bundle is using a seat license, they should **NOT**activate the license at this time so that the employees can activate the seat license key on their own computers. A floating license is a more convenient solution for large companies. For more information about licensing, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Modeling tools and plugins licensing' space=''] page.
4. Install the required plugins. For more information, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing plugins' space=''] and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Resource Manager' space='MD2024x'] pages. Make sure not to close the modeling tool after this step, as additional configuration changes are needed.
5. Specify all necessary environment options ( Options > Environment Options ). For the Environment Options dialog description, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Customizing environment options' space='MD2024x'] page. The most important environment options are:
  1. Security certificates to enable secure communication between the modeling tool and Teamwork Cloud. Follow the steps at the bottom of the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Enabling secure connection between client and server' space='TWCloud2024x'] page.
  2. Floating License Server information .
    1. Connect to the Floating License server and check out a license. When the person building the bundle connects to the license server successfully, the server’s name and port are set in the corresponding properties of the **Environment Options** > **Floating**section.
    2. Select the check box Auto Login to the License Server (the user can reset this setting later and select the licenses manually if needed).
  3. Teamwork Cloud Server information.
    1. In the Environment Options, click Collaboration .
    2. Select the **Server Name** and check the appropriate security choices for your deployment environment. When the person building the bundle connects to Teamwork Cloud successfully, the server’s name and the user name used to connect will be set in the Environment Options. If the person building the bundle does not want their user name to be part of the bundle, they should not connect to Teamwork Cloud before finishing the bundle. Instead, just set the Environment Options as described above.
  4. Cameo Collaborator Server information.
    1. In the Environment Options, click on Cameo Collaborator .
    2. Set the Cameo Collaborator URL.
6. Close the modeling tool.
7. Open the modeling tool (this step is mandatory if any plugins were installed during Step 4).
  1. Verify that all plugins are installed.
    1. In the Main Menu, click Help > Resource/Plugin Manager . Check if all needed plugins are marked as 'Installed'.
  2. Verify Environment Options.
    1. In the Main Menu, click Options > Environment Options and check if your settings are saved.
8. Close the modeling tool.
9. **If you want the configuration directory to be back at the default location, which is under the Users directory in Windows, then the changes made in Step 2 will need to be changed back:**** For employees to get the bundle with the predefined configuration options, the configuration files should be located in the installation folder, which is generally located in the *C:\Program Files*directory. However, since the Program Files folder is often read-only on users' business computers and the users do not have the write permissions, moving the configuration directory is very common, and so the default location for storing various configuration files is *C:\Users\<your username>\AppData\Local\.<modeling_tool_name>\<version_number>.*For more information about the configuration files' location, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] page.
  1. In the <modeling tool installation>/bin folder, open the <modeling_tool_name> .properties file.
  2. Change the -DLOCALCONFIG option value to true : -DLOCALCONFIG\=true
  3. Remove -DWINCONFIG\=false
  4. Save the *<modeling_tool_name>**.properties* file. Now, once an employee starts the modeling tool, all the configuration files will be located in the *C:\Users\<your username>\AppData\Local\.<modeling_tool_name>\<version number>***directory.** Do not launch the bundle that is being built after this step. After step 9.d, if the person building the bundle launches the bundle, then the configuration directory will no longer be in the installation directory. This will cause the final bundle not to work correctly. Wait until after Step 11, create the zip file, copy the zip file to another directory, and then extract it.
10. Change the Java path if needed. The modeling tool's *installer.exe* file installs bundled Java to the modeling tool's installation directory, which will be used by default. Copying the installation folder to another computer will copy the Java VM, too. Thus, the employee will not be required to install Java manually. For this reason, we recommend using the bundled Java. 
However, if the bundle is prepared using the no installer file (*<modeling_tool_name>_<version number>_no_install.zip*), which does not contain Java, the Java path in the *properties* file is empty, so Java needs to be installed on the employee's computer separately, and its path needs to be specified manually. To check which Java version is used by the modeling tool, go to the MagicDraw **Help**menu > **About MagicDraw**> **Environment** tab. 
To check the recommended Java version for your tool, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Java version support' space='NMDOC'] page. To specify the Java path:
  1. Determine the path where Java will be installed on the end user’s computer.
  2. In the <modeling tool installation>\bin folder, open the <modeling_tool_name> .properties file.
  3. Locate the line JAVA_HOME= and change the path to JAVA_HOME=<Path to the directory where Java is installed on an employee's computer>
  4. Save the <modeling_tool_name> .properties file.
11. Compress the installation folder (you can use .zip , .rar, or any other format). You have now prepared the modeling tools bundle with already installed plugins and predefined options.

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726271 space=IL2024x version=2 -->
## PAGE 00017: Determine the Host ID or Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed

- page_id: `136726271`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726271/Determine+the+Host+ID+or+Target+ID+of+the+machine+on+which+the+FlexNet+license+server+is+installed
- version_number: 2
- version_date: `2024-11-14T09:14:25.206+01:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing > Adding a license to the FlexNet server
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

INLINE

If you do not have FlexNet yet, you can [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading Reader installation files' space=''] containing [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='3DS Media list for Readers 2024x' space=''], allowing you to set up FlexNet.

You can determine the Host ID/Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed:

- using .
- using **.** FlexNet license server supports only one Host ID/Target ID.

###### lmadminTo determine the Host ID/Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed (using *lmadmin*)

1. Connect to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface. The default address is[http://localhost:8090](http://localhost:8090/)or use your server name (*http://<server name>:8090*).
2. Click **Administration** at the top-right corner of the webpage. When prompted to sign in, enter the default administrator's credentials (*admin*/*admin)*.
3. Copy the Host ID/Target ID displayed as Ethernet Address (as in the following figure). [ATTACHMENT filename='ethernet_address.png']

###### lmhostidTo determine the Host ID/Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed (using *lmhostid*)

The *lmhostid* is a command line utility, which prints the Host ID/Target ID that a FlexNet license server requires on any supported system. The *Lmhostid* utility is available as an executable called *lmutil*.

1. Locate lmutil for a particular OS in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''] <*product folder*>\Flex_Utilities_User_Guides_Vendor_Daemons\<*FlexNet version*>\Server utilities folder.
2. Run lmutil with lmhostid parameter from the command line. Lmhostid displays the default Host ID/Target ID for the current platform.

For the exact commands for a specific OS refer to: License Administration Guide (Obtaining System Hostids):

- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.18.2.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf']

If two or more Ethernet addresses are available on the particular machine, the first one printed by the Host ID command should be used.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<ac:structured-macro ac:name="excerpt" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="36b4b5a5-4fe9-45fc-97f2-adce56beb839"><ac:parameter ac:name="atlassian-macro-output-type">INLINE</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><ac:structured-macro ac:name="tip" ac:schema-version="1" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[download the free Reader installation files]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> containing <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="3DS Media list for Readers 2024x" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[FlexNet utilities]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link>, allowing you to set up FlexNet.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p>You can determine the Host ID.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></li></ul><h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="76aec613-3f11-4b11-bdbb-9d094cdb51b5"><ac:parameter /><ol><li><p><span style="color: rgb(35,35,35);">Connect to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface.</span></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="6c8af5c7-000c-4391-94df-92e77515cc79"><ac:rich-text-body><p><span style="color: rgb(35,35,35);">The default address is  </span><a class="external-link" href="http://localhost:8090/" rel="nofollow">http://localhost:8090</a><span style="color: rgb(35,35,35);"> or use your server name (</span><em>http://&lt;server name&gt;:8090</em><span style="color: rgb(35,35,35);">).</span></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></li><li><p>Click <strong>Administration</strong> at the top-right corner of the webpage. When prompted to sign in, enter the default administrator's credentials (<em>admin</em>/<em>admin)</em>.</p></li><li>Copy the Host ID/Target ID displayed as Ethernet Address (as in the following figure).<br /><ac:image ac:title="Ethernet Address of the machine on which the FlexNet server is installed" ac:alt="Ethernet Address of the machine on which the FlexNet server is installed" ac:height="479" ac:width="618"><ri:attachment ri:filename="ethernet_address.png" /></ac:image></li></ol><p><br /></p><h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="1e0b2e96-2cc2-4157-ac97-0b3815f96c3d"><ac:parameter ac:name="">lmhostid</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>To determine the Host ID/Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed (using <em>lmhostid</em>)</h4><p>The <em>lmhostid</em> is a command line utility, which prints the Host ID/Target ID that a FlexNet license server requires on any supported system. The <em>Lmhostid</em> utility is available as an executable called <em>lmutil</em>. </p><hr /><ol><li>Locate <em>lmutil</em> for a particular OS in the <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Downloading installation files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[downloaded]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> <strong>&lt;<em>product folder</em>&gt;\Flex_Utilities_User_Guides_Vendor_Daemons\&lt;<em>FlexNet version</em>&gt;\Server utilities</strong> folder.</li><li>Run <em>lmutil</em> with <em>lmhostid</em> parameter from the command line. <em>Lmhostid</em> displays the default Host ID/Target ID for the current platform.</li></ol><p><br /></p><p>For the exact commands for a specific OS refer to: License Administration Guide (Obtaining System Hostids):</p><ul><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2022 R1 (11.19.0)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11.18.2.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2021 R3 (11.18.2)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2020 R2 (11.17.0)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2019 R2 (11.16.4)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li><li><ac:link><ri:attachment ri:filename="fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf"><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ri:attachment><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[License Administration Guide. FlexNet Publisher 2014 R1 (11.12.1)]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="e88f068a-9fea-4893-be5d-2e1c255a716b"><ac:rich-text-body><p>If two or more Ethernet addresses are available on the particular machine, the first one printed by the Host ID command should be used.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p>
````

## PAGE 00018: Determine the Target ID

- page_id: `136726217`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726217/Determine+the+Target+ID
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:19.328+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Modeling tools and plugins licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

To determine the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Basic concepts' space='IL2024x'] of the machine on which the modeling tool is installed

1. Start the modeling tool.
2. When the License Manager dialog opens, click Show Target ID .
3. Select one of the following tabs based on the license server you want to use:
  1. FlexNet . Click to copy the text from the Host ID box.
  2. **DSLS**. Click to copy the text from the **Computer ID** box. Please note that more than one Target ID may be shown if you have several network adapters. [IMAGE alt='' src='']

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE


## PAGE 00019: Downloading installation files

- page_id: `136726112`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726112/Downloading+installation+files
- version_number: 6
- version_date: `2025-05-16T09:35:00.418+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

##### 3DS Media lists

The topics below contain detailed lists of all the contents of the installation bundles for specific product versions, along with respective file locations.

The following list is not a full list of our product releases and the topics in the list do not contain links to software downloads. Use the topics below as a guide when you are not sure which installation bundle to download.

true

For the media list for Readers, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading Reader installation files' space='ILTWRT'].

##### How to download your software

The installation files are available on the 3DS software download page[https://www.3ds.com/support/download/](https://www.3ds.com/support/download/).

If you do not have access to the 3DS software download page, please contact your sales representative.

To access your download page

1. Login to https://software.3ds.com/ with your [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='3DEXPERIENCE ID creation and validation' space='NMDOC'] . By default, you will be redirected to **My Supported Software** .
2. Select CATIA brand.
3. Select No Magic product line. [ATTACHMENT filename='Step3_download_page_updated_pic.jpg']
4. Select Release (e.g. major version) and Level (e.g service pack) and Hot Fixes (if available).
5. Browse for required media files and click **Show details.** To find out the content of the volumes, refer to the [3DS Media list](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/IL2024xR2/3DS+Media+list+for+2024x+Refresh2+release) page.
6. Click the download button or select the required volume file to start the download. [ATTACHMENT filename='Step6_picture_updated.jpg']

#### EXPAND: Up to 2021x

Up to 2021x

If you have No Magic login credentials, you can access the installation files, including the FlexNet license server utilities as well as the Demo and Reader versions of the modeling tool, at [nomagic.com](https://www.3ds.com/products-services/catia/products/no-magic/).

To proceed, click [IMAGE alt='' src=''].

## PAGE 00020: Downloading Reader installation files

- page_id: `143394386`
- space_key: `IL2024x`

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

To download the installation files

1. Go to https://software.3ds.com/ and do one of the following:
  - Log in to the site if you have your **3D**EXPERIENCE ID .
  - Create an account if you do not have the 3D EXPERIENCE ID.
2. At the top of the page, click Free Download . [ATTACHMENT filename='reader_download_1.png']
3. Click CATIA Magic / No Magic . [ATTACHMENT filename='reader_download_2.png']
4. In the open window, read the license agreement and click the Accept the license agreement button if you want to continue.
5. Select Release (e.g. major version) and Level (e.g service pack). [ATTACHMENT filename='reader_download_3.png']
6. In the needed media files line, click **Show details**. The content of the media files is listed in the table below. To find out the content of the volumes, refer to the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='3DS Media list for Readers 2024x' space=''] page.
7. Click the download button or select the required volume file to start the download. [ATTACHMENT filename='reader_download_4.png']

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726243 space=IL2024x version=12 -->
## PAGE 00021: DSLS installation and licensing

- page_id: `136726243`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726243/DSLS+installation+and+licensing
- version_number: 12
- version_date: `2024-05-15T15:21:08.694+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

DSLS (Dassault Systèmes License Server) is a licensing system developed by Dassault Systèmes that provides such benefits as:

- License usage statistics, debugging, and simple UI to administer and view statistics.
- Licenses are bound to expiration date rather than product version.
- Nodelock, floating, and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Managed licensing' space=''] licensing options.

##### DSLS and modeling tools compatibility

You **must** choose the DSLS version compatible with the modeling tool version you use.

| Modeling tool | DSLS version | Compatible |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 2024x | R2024x |  |

* To run DSLS 2024x licensing on Linux, glibc 3.4.20 (at a minimum) is required.

****IMPORTANT**. To use modeling tools with DSLS licenses,Microsoft Visual C++ Redistributable must be installed (see[Latest supported Visual C++ Redistributable downloads](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/cpp/windows/latest-supported-vc-redist?view=msvc-170#visual-studio-2015-2017-2019-and-2022)). This applies to Windows OS only.

##### DSLS hosting restrictions

- DSLS servers can only be hosted on physical computers (with the exception of using HyperV virtualization; see the [Installation Guide](http://media.3ds.com/support/documentation/product/DS_License_Server/R2024x/DSLS-installation-and-configuration-guide.pdf?_gl=1*zecu5a*_ga*MjA1MDE4MDI3LjE2NjkwMTM5OTY.*_ga_DYJDKXYEZ4*MTcwMDEyMzUxMS40OS4wLjE3MDAxMjM1MTEuNjAuMC4w)).

##### DSLS licensing client-side main limitations

###### Supported license types

- Client on a physical machine - floating (online), floating (offline/borrowed), nodelock.
- Client on a virtual machine - floating (online).

- Offline (borrowed) licenses are not supported on macOS/Linux.

More information can be found in the DSLS server [Installation Guide](http://media.3ds.com/support/documentation/product/DS_License_Server/R2024x/DSLS-installation-and-configuration-guide.pdf?_gl=1*zecu5a*_ga*MjA1MDE4MDI3LjE2NjkwMTM5OTY.*_ga_DYJDKXYEZ4*MTcwMDEyMzUxMS40OS4wLjE3MDAxMjM1MTEuNjAuMC4w).

##### Product trigrams

With DSLS, product licenses are checked out using trigrams instead of the full product name. To know the specific trigrams denoting each product, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Product trigrams' space=''] page.

##### Detailed licensing information

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining License Keys' space='']
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Modeling tools and plugins licensing' space='']

##### 3DS DSLS installation guide and software keys

- DSLS Installation and Configuration Guide
- Dassault Systèmes License Server and License Keys
- Software License Keys

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE


<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726259 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00022: FlexNet license server 11.12, 11.14, 11.16

- page_id: `136726259`
- space_key: `IL2024x`

##### Choosing the Flexnet server manager

There are three types of FlexNet server managers:

- *lmadmin* – a web-based license server manager with GUI (recommended).
- *lmgrd* – a license server manager with a command-line interface.
- *lmtools –*the old Windows-based server manager (replaced by*lmadmin*).

We recommend using *lmadmin*.

- lmadmin installer comes in 32-bit architecture (regardless of the version) only.
- 11.12.1 version license server utilities (except the lmadmin installer) come in 32/64-bit architectures.
- 11.14 version license tools are not available in 64-bit binaries. Only 32-bit tools are available (additional 32-bit libraries need to be installed in the 64-bit multi-arch system to execute them).

##### Prerequisites

- You have [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''] the installation files of:
  - the FlexNet license server manager.
  - the vendor daemon - Cameo.

The license server manager (e.g., *l**madmin*) should be of the same or later version as a vendor daemon - Cameo you use.

##### For **Windows**users

To use *lmadmin* on Windows platforms, the Microsoft Visual C++ 2013 Redistributable Package must be installed. You have an option to install this package during the FlexNet Publisher License Server Installer process.

| Windows | 32-bit system | 64-bit system |
| --- | --- | --- |
| You can run lmadmin (11.12.1) on these officially supported platforms:Windows 8Windows Server 2012Windows Server 2008Windows 7 (Ultimate)Windows Vista (Ultimate)You can run lmadmin (11.14) on these officially supported platforms:Windows 10Windows Server 2008, including SP1, SP2, and R2Windows 8Windows 8.1Windows 7, including SP1Windows Server 2012 R2Windows Server 2012 | We recommend using 32-bit lmadmin or 32-bit lmgrd with a 32-bit Cameo daemon vendor file. | We recommend using 32-bit lmadmin. Additional 32-bit libraries need to be installed in the 64-bit multi-arch system to execute them. |

##### For**Linux** users

| Linux | 32-bit system | 64-bit system |
| --- | --- | --- |
| You need to have the glibc libraries installed corresponding to your operating system architecture.You need to create a non-root system user with root privileges and install/run the server tools using it:This can be achieved either by:1. Adding the user to the 'sudo' group2. Editing the file /etc/sudoers using visudo.Method 1 (Ubuntu based)Method 2 (Ubuntu based)Method 1 (Redhat/Fedora/CentOS) | We recommend using the 32-bit lmadmin installer or 32-bit lmgrd. You need to install the Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.For UbuntuFor Redhat/CentOS/Fedora | We recommended using 32-bit lmadmin and 64-bit lmgrd for 64-bit multi-arch systems.For version 11.12.1 we recommend either using the 32-bit lmadmin installer (for multi-arch systems), or the 64-bit lmgrd:Installing 32-bit lmadmin on a multi-arch machine will require 32-bit libraries.For recent UbuntuFor older Ubuntu useFor Redhat/CentOS/FedoraRunning 64-bit lmgrd on 64-bit systems requires 64-bit Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.For UbuntuFor Redhat/CentOS/FedoraFor version 11.14 we recommend either using the 32-bit lmadmin installer, or the 32-bit lmgrd for multi-arch systems. 64-bit 11.14 lmadmin/lmgrd binaries are not available.Both of them require 32-bit libraries. Install it using:For recent UbuntuFor older UbuntuFor Redhat/CentOS/Fedoralmadmin 11.14 comes with libssl.so.1.0.0 in its installation directory.You need to add these libraries in lmadmin directory to the LD_LIBRARY_PATH in order to run lmadmin.e.g. if your lmadmin installation is at /opt/FNPLicenseServerManager then adding it to the path would look like this: |

#### EXCERPT: Method 2 (Ubuntu based)

INLINE

##### Choosing the Flexnet server manager

There are three types of FlexNet server managers:

- *lmadmin* – a web-based license server manager with GUI (recommended).
- *lmgrd* – a license server manager with a command-line interface.
- *lmtools –*the old Windows-based server manager (replaced by*lmadmin*).

We recommend using *lmadmin*.

##### Prerequisites

- You have [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''] the installation files of:
  - the FlexNet license server manager.
  - the vendor daemon - Cameo.

The license server manager (e.g., *l**madmin*) should be of the same or later version as a vendor daemon - Cameo you use.

##### Windows

To use *lmadmin* on Windows platforms, the Microsoft Visual C++ 2013 Redistributable Package must be installed. You have an option to install this package during the FlexNet Publisher License Server Installer process.

| Modeling tool version | 32-bit system | 64-bit system |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 2021x and later | We recommend using 32-bit lmadmin or 32-bit lmgrd with a 32-bit Cameo daemon vendor file. | We recommend using 64-bit lmadmin or 64-bit lmgrd with a 64-bit Cameo daemon vendor file. |
| 19.0 and earlier | We recommend using 32-bit lmadmin or 32-bit lmgrd with a 32-bit Cameo daemon vendor file. | We recommend using 32-bit lmadmin or 32-bit lmgrd with a 64-bit Cameo daemon vendor file. |

**[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing FlexNet 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0' space='']**

##### Linux

It is the best practice to run license servers on a server-based OS.

- You need to have the glibc libraries installed corresponding to your operating system architecture.
- You need to create a non-root system user with root privileges and install/run the server tools(lmadmin/lmgrd) using it.
- You need to install the Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.

**Redhat/Fedora/CentOS**

1. Create a new user and add this user to the group.

2. Add user to sudoers (/etc/sudoers).

3. Install the Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.

```text
> /etc/sudoers
sudo yum install -y ld-linux.so.2
sudo yum install redhat-lsb-core]]>
```

Check if LSB was successfully installed using:

```text

```

In order to query which LSB library is required for a particular Centos version, the following command can be executed:

```text

```

**Ubuntu OS**

1. Add the user to the 'sudo' group

2. Edit the file /etc/sudoers using visudo.

```text

```

```text

```

3. Install the Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.

```text

```

| Modeling tool version | 32-bit system | 64-bit system |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 2021x and later | We recommend using 32-bit lmadmin installer or 32-bit lmgrd. | We recommend using 64-bit lmadmin or 64-bit lmgrd with a 64-bit Cameo daemon vendor file. |
| 19.0 and earlier | We recommend using 32-bit lmadmin installer or 32-bit lmgrd. | Please use 32-bit lmadmin installer. Additional 32-bit libraries need to be installed in the 64-bit multi-arch system to execute them.Alternatively, you can use 64-bit lmgrd version 11.12.1. >]]> |

Cameo you use.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><h3 class="auto-cursor-target">Windows</h3><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="036ce8ad-72ca-4f4e-8dcc-e3cbcb0edccf"><ac:rich-text-body><p>To use <em>lmadmin</em> on Windows platforms, the Microsoft Visual C++ 2013 Redistributable Package must be installed. ac:name="info" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="9c226d4b-63d4-4f96-af9b-f6ac20daf7b0"><ac:rich-text-body><p>It is the best practice to run license servers on a server-based OS.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ul><li>You need to have the <em>glibc</em> libraries installed corresponding to your operating system architecture.</li><li class="auto-cursor-target"><p>You need to create a non-root system user with root privileges and install/run the server tools(lmadmin/lmgrd) using it.</p></li><li class="auto-cursor-target"><p><span>You need to install the Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.</span></p></li></ul><p><strong>Redhat/Fedora/CentOS</strong></p><p>1. Create a new user and add this user to the group.</p><p>2. Add user to sudoers (/etc/sudoers).</p><p>3. <span>Install the Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.</span></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="095b902b-38ab-4905-bd3f-2827fb67f50e"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Redhat/Fedora/CentOS</ac:parameter><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[sudo groupadd -r lmadmin
````html
sudo useradd -d /home/lmadmin -g lmadmin -m -r lmadmin
sudo echo "lmadmin ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL " >> /etc/sudoers
sudo yum install -y ld-linux.so.2
sudo yum install redhat-lsb-core]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p>Check if LSB was successfully installed using:</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="e6aaa2d3-43a3-4dae-91d1-2725008c240a"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[lsb_release -a]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="9a3016a3-215c-478e-9b3b-4718b118c6ea"><ac:rich-text-body><p>In order to query which LSB library is required for a particular Centos version, the following command can be executed:</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="2da32215-dd17-4353-a492-aaa69c96c8a8"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[sudo yum provides /lib/ld-lsb.so.3]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p><strong>Ubuntu OS</strong></p><p>1. Add the user to the 'sudo' group</p><p>2. Edit the file /etc/sudoers using visudo.</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="2ba8d9ea-6775-4314-bd7d-4d932d3de324"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Method 1 (Ubuntu based)</ac:parameter><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[sudo adduser newuser
sudo usermod -aG sudo newuser]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="7cca31eb-a3fb-4e77-b4be-f3002264a5f1"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Method 2 (Ubuntu based)</ac:parameter><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[Modify '/etc/sudoers' with the editor "visudo".

#Create a user called "newuser"
[root@mylinux~]#useradd newuser
[root@mylinux~]#passwd newuser

#Edit the file with visudo:
[root@mylinux~]# visudo

#Find a line 'User privilege specification' and add the following.
newuser ALL=(ALL) ALL]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p>3. I<span>nstall the Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.<br /></span></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ## PAGE 00024: FlexNet license server installation and licensing
````

- page_id: `136726245`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726245/FlexNet+license+server+installation+and+licensing
- version_number: 3
- version_date: `2024-08-26T07:41:24.134+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

474485234

474485237

474485233

INLINE

**On this page**

**Related resources**

- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.18.2.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf']

474485236

INLINE

The FlexNet Publisher license server (the floating license server) from [Flexera](https://www.flexera.com/) is used for managing floating licenses. The basic components of the FlexNet Publisher license server are these:

- license server administrator
- license key file
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Basic concepts' space='']

A floating license allows you to install and use the same licenseon multiple machines.The licenses are managed by the floating license server. The floating license server has information on the total number of products and editions you have and how many of these licenses are currently in use.

##### Getting the FlexNet license server installation files

In your 'FlexNet License Server utilities' folder, you can find the FlexNet license server installation files, Administration user guides, and release notes. The folder is located in the appropriate media volume. To find out, which media volume contains the 'FlexNet License Server utilities' folder, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''] based on the release version.

[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space='']>]]>

##### Using the FlexNet license server

To use the FlexNet server

1. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing FlexNet 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0' space='']
2. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding a license to the FlexNet server' space=''] .

##### modeling tool and flexnet compatibilityFlexNet server and modeling tools compatibility

You need to choose the version of the **FlexNet license server** and a **vendor daemon - Cameo** according to the modeling tool version you use.

| Modeling tool\FlexNet version | 11.12.0 and below | 11.14.0 | 11.16.4 | 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 2021x and later | not compatible | X 1 | X 1 | X |
| 19.0 and earlier | X | X 1 | X 1 | X 1 |

1 Windows 64-bit, Linux 64-bit, and MAC 64-bit ***lmadmin*\*lmgrd*** are incompatible with a**vendor daemons – *cameo*** of 64-bit. 
Use ***32-bit*** ***lmadmin*** according to instructions for [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server 11.12, 11.14, 11.16' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0' space='']

FlexNet license borrowing is not supported on macOS machines running with ARM Java.

## PAGE 00025: FlexNet Three-Server Redundancy - Triad License Server

- page_id: `136726276`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726276/FlexNet+Three-Server+Redundancy+-+Triad+License+Server
- version_number: 3
- version_date: `2025-01-31T13:08:02.083+01:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**On this page**

5

Using the three-server redundancy capability in FlexNet Publisher, all three license servers operate to form a triad. The license servers send periodic messages to each other to make sure that at least two servers are running and communicating. A quorum is formed when at least two of the three license servers are running and communicating with each other. For more information, see the FlexNet Administration Guide on the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server installation and licensing' space=''] page.

Teamwork Cloud and Magic Collaboration Studio do not support Triad License Server.

##### Prerequisites

In order to run a license server in a Three-Server Redundancy mode (Triad License Server), you must first obtain a license key suited for it.

The license key must contain 3 SERVER lines with *hostnames* and MAC addresses defined.

##### Starting on a fresh installation of *lmadmin*

1. Have the cameo daemon in <lmadmin.install.dir>\licenses\cameo
2. The first server from the license key should be started first, by importing the license key from the lmadmin Administration tab.
3. After the import, the cameo daemon will state that it is "Down", and the lmadmin.log file will be displayed. This will happen until the second server is started.

```text

```

Licenses will only be served when there are at least 2 license servers running.

##### Starting on a *lmadmin* that was running a single license server

If *lmadmin* was previously started with a different, single server license, there is additional action needed. By starting a single license server, it goes into a single license server mode, and thus won't accept Three-Server redundancy (Triad) license keys.

There are two options:

- Do a clean installation of lmadmin.
- Reconfigure the current lmadmin and change the license mode.

###### Clean installation

To do a clean installation of *lmadmin*, first, you need to remove the previous installation. Then you can proceed with the fresh installation (see ).

###### Reconfigure the current *lmadmin*

Reconfigure the current *lmadmin* and change the license mode:

Steps to change server mode:

```text

```

1. Start lmadmin (using service). You do not need to do anything else after that. It will show Stopped until a quorum is reached (then it will start). Licenses will be served only when there are at least 2 servers running lmadmin (from the 3 defined).
2. The log file lmadmin.log , will show:

```text

```

- Make sure the license server is using a defined port, the same one as defined in the license file.
- Three-server redundancy configurations require all three servers to use the same platform type.

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726183 space=IL2024x version=4 -->
## PAGE 00026: Floating licensing

- page_id: `136726183`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726183/Floating+licensing
- version_number: 4
- version_date: `2023-11-30T12:05:20.811+01:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Sales and licenses
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

1243258352

1243258373

1243258351

**On this page**

1243258362

##### What is Floating Licensing?

FL (Floating License) allows you to install and use the same license (i.e. MagicDraw Standard, Professional, Enterprise Edition or Plugins) on multiple machines. Suppose you have 10 workstations where MagicDraw is used. In most cases there are less than 10 users concurrently using MagicDraw. Instead of purchasing 10 Professional (or Standard) seat licenses, only purchase the number of Floating Licenses to support the number of concurrent users. Floating License(s) are usually more economical in development centers than purchasing individual seat licenses.

##### How does license server works?

Whenever you obtain Floating License you may install MagicDraw client application (Standard - Enterprise) on as many workstations as you need. The license server software (which is free and is provided together with FL clients) needs to be installed on some computer (which is referred to as a license server). Normally, only one license server is required in your network.

The license server is provided with the key, which specifies how many and what types of Floating Licenses this server may serve. The same server may serve different numbers of different Editions and plugins licenses, e.g. 2 Standard and 3 Professional FL licenses. In this case, during the connection, you will be asked to select the edition you want to run - Standard, Enterprise, or Professional.

##### How does a client application obtain the floating license?

In order to work with the FL client, you will need to specify the address of the license server and port (by default, FlexNet - 1101, DSLS - 4085) and connect to it. Every time FL client connects to the license server it checked out a license from that server and the number of available licenses on this server is decreased. If all available licenses from the server are leased, the next client who wants to obtain a license must wait until one of the other client's finishes its work and the license is returned back to the license server.

##### What if the connection with the license server is lost?

Whenever FL client leases the license from the license server, it constantly updates the server with the message that it is still alive. The license server in turn acknowledges that the license is still valid. If the connection with the server is lost, the client application will not receive acknowledgements from the server and the client application will be gracefully terminated (MagicDraw forces you to save your work and close the application or try to reconnect again). In the case of no update from the client, the license server considers the license to be returned and it is available to other clients.

##### Floating licenses on a Laptop

Floating Licenses are primarily intended for workstations directly connected to a network. However, a portable computer that is connected to the Internet and can contact the license server, may use a Floating License as well.

##### Borrowing - offline license mode

If a license will to be used on a computer that is intermittently connected to the license server, that license can be borrowed from server and used as an offline floating license. A license can be borrowed from a license server for the selected period of time (default 24 hours) via Select Edition/Plugin in application. The borrowed license is used as an application on a computer that is no longer connected to the license server.

##### Node locking

Floating licenses are locked to a particular machine, on which the FLEXnet/DSLS server is running. The Ethernet address (also referred to as a MAC address) of Ethernet devices or NICs (network interface cards) is used as the Target ID for server license locking to particular hardware.

##### DSLS license server

For detailed information regarding DSLS, see the [DSLS Installation and Configuration Guide](http://media.3ds.com/support/documentation/product/DS_License_Server/2023x/DSLS_Installation_and_Configuration_Guide_23x.pdf?_gl=1*1b9rvxw*_ga*MjA1MDE4MDI3LjE2NjkwMTM5OTY.*_ga_DYJDKXYEZ4*MTY5MzIyODIzOS4zMi4wLjE2OTMyMjgyMzkuNjAuMC4w).

##### FLEXnet license server

###### License Server Manager

FLEXnet license server is used to manage floating licenses. The license server manager is one of the components that makes up a license server (the other being the vendor daemon). There is available a Web-based license server manager with the graphical user interface (GUI) - lmadmin.

A brief FLEXnet license server advantages and capabilities:

- Intuitive license management with rich graphical user interface provided by lmadmin.
- Easy to perform general license management tasks, such as configuring license and stopping servers.
- Easy accessible picture of license status - how many licenses are available and who is using them.
- Ability to report on the duration a product is in use.
- Alerts if licenses are running low, unavailable, etc.
- Allow/deny/reserve products to be used by specific users, hosts, and groups.
- Log file is generated, containing products usage information.

###### Structure of FLEXnet license server

*Vendor daemon* - one of the files that is a part of the license server. This executable is customized and built by us. To serve our products licenses, license server requires cameo vendor daemon.

*License file* - a text file, usually with the .lic or .txt extension, which contains license certificates.

*Options file* - a configuration file available on the license server, which license administrators can use to allow / deny / reserve products to be used by specific users, hosts, and groups.

*Report log file* - a file that runs on a license server, which contains data about the features used by a single vendor daemon. Report logs are encrypted and cannot be read by a person, but are used by FLEXnet Manager to produce reports.

*Debug log file* - a file used by the license server to record status and error messages that are useful for debugging the license server. Each license server can have one or more of these files.

*lmadmin* - the new license server manager, which includes a Web-based GUI.

*lmgrd* - a command-line-based license server manager.

###### License usage analysis

FLEXnet Manager is the only official solution with the direct access to the FLEX license usage information – enabling enterprises to track and manage their FLEXenabled software with the most comprehensive and accurate usage reports.

Use Flexera Software license administration solution, FLEXnet Manager, to gain exceptional visibility into license usage data and to create insightful reports on critical information like license availability and usage. FLEXnet Manager can be fully automated to run these reports on schedule and can be used to track license servers and usage across a heterogeneous network of server including Windows NT, Linux and UNIX. Contact Flexera Software at [www.flexerasoftware.com](http://www.flexerasoftware.com) for more details on how to obtain an evaluation copy of FLEXnet Manager for your enterprise.

In order to track license usage and gather license related statistics you might consider third party software also:

[http://www.openlm.com](http://www.openlm.com/) 
[http://www.jtbworld.com/jtbflexreport/index.htm](http://www.jtbworld.com/jtbflexreport/index.htm) 
[https://www.x-formation.com/license-statistics](https://www.x-formation.com/license-statistics)

###### Server configuration capabilities

The License Server options file allows the license administrator to control various operating parameters within the constraints of the license model. The user is identified by his/her user name, host name, display, IP address, and other. For the concurrent (floating) licenses, the license administrator can perform the following actions:

- Allow / deny / reserve products to be used by specific users, hosts, and groups.
- Restrict the number of licenses available.

For more information, see "Managing the Options File" section in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0' space=''].

###### Server alerts

The license server alerts when there are no available licenses or the server is down.

Alerts are configurable. You may set up lmadmin to issue alerts and warn you of potential problems. For example, you may set up to get alerts on license expiry or vendor daemon status.

Optionally you may use an lmadmin email alerter service. This service will poll for alerts and then send a user an email when an alert has been triggered.

For more information, see "Creating an lmadmin Alerter Service section" in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0' space=''].

###### References

[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server installation and licensing' space='']

[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0' space='']

## PAGE 00027: How to change JVM version

- page_id: `249579961`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/249579961/How+to+change+JVM+version
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2025-09-02T14:08:03.107+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Java version support
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

To change JVM version

1. Go to <modeling tool installation directory>\bin and open the <modeling tool>.properties file (eg., magicdraw.properties , csm.properties , cameoea.properties ) for editing. If you are using MagicDraw 17.0.4 or earlier, the name of the property file is mduml.properties .
2. In the JAVA_HOME line, add the path to the Java software. For example: JAVA_HOME=C\:\\Program Files\\Java\\jre1.8.0_144

integrations

````html
<p>To change JVM version</p><hr /><ol><li>Go to <em>&lt;modeling tool installation directory&gt;\bin</em> and open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.properties</em> file (eg., <em>magicdraw.properties</em>, <em>csm.properties</em>, <em>cameoea.properties</em>) for editing. If you are using MagicDraw 17.0.4 or earlier, the name of the property file is <em>mduml.properties</em>.</li><li>In the JAVA_HOME line, add the path to the Java software. For example: JAVA_HOME=C\:\\Program Files\\Java\\jre1.8.0_144</li></ol><p><br /></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="4e32030a-21c0-4de2-9f7f-49e2466f3a2c"><ac:rich-text-body>Integrated MagicDraw runs on the JVM specified by the IDE. In order to change the JVM, you must modify the startup properties for the IDE that MagicDraw integrates with. ## PAGE 00030: Installing FlexNet 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0
````

- page_id: `136726256`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726256/Installing+FlexNet+11.17.0+11.18.2+11.19.0
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:20.938+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing > FlexNet license server 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### CONTENT-LAYER: For OS X and Linux users

1081072676

#### CONTENT-COLUMN: For OS X and Linux users

1081072697

1081072674

**On this page**

#### CONTENT-BLOCK: For OS X and Linux users

1081072686

#### EXCERPT: For OS X and Linux users

INLINE

##### Installation procedure

###### For Windows

1. Install the FlexNet license server manager. We highly recommend running the FlexNet license server (*lmadmin*) as a service (on Windows).As a result, the server can start automatically after the machine boots. Starting the server manually is not user-friendly – there is no GUI for this action.If your operating system is Windows, you only need to select the **Run as a service** check box when prompted during the *lmadmin* installation.[IMAGE alt='' src='']For the instructions on how to create a daemon, refer to Automatic Start in:[ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf'][ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_18_2.pdf'][ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf']
2. Place the vendor daemon - Cameo into the FlexNet server install folder. If you use *lmadmin*, do the following: [IMAGE alt='' src=''] Note that all files in *install* and *data (for Windows)* dirs must have read/write permissions. *lmadmin* or cameo daemon may not start even if a log file or cameo daemon does not have r/w permissions.Use this command to set permissions for all files within the directory recursively.chmod -R 755 FNPLicenseServerManager
  1. Open the FlexNet server install folder.
  2. In the install folder, create the licenses\cameo folder.
  3. Place the Vendor daemon in *<FlexNet server data folder>\licenses\cameo*.
3. Start the server (as a service), or using the command line manually by running the *lmadmin* file from the FlexNet server installation directory. Running lmadmin using command line on WindowsIf a service was not installed and you want to run your lmadmin using command line, you will have to define the additional required parameters. e.g. -configDir. The dir is located in your *data* dir (for example *C:\ProgramData\FLEXlm\lmadmin or any other location you defined while installing).*

###### For Linux

1. Install the FlexNet license server manager. We highly recommend running the FlexNet license server (*lmadmin*) as a daemon (on OS X or Linux).As a result, the server can start automatically after the machine boots. Starting the server manually is not user-friendly – there is no GUI for this action.For the instructions on how to create a daemon, refer to Automatic Start in:[ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf'][ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_18_2.pdf'][ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf']
2. Place the vendor daemon - Cameo into the FlexNet server install folder. If you use *lmadmin*, do the following:
  1. Open the FlexNet server install folder. For OS X and Linux usersIf you don't have permission to open the FlexNet server data folder, execute the following command from the root:On OS X 
chmod g+x FNPLicenseServerManager/ 
chmod –R g+w ./*On Linuxchmod g+x FNPLicenseServerManager/
  2. In the install folder, create the licenses\cameo folder.
  3. Place the Vendor daemon in *<FlexNet server data folder>\licenses\cameo*.
3. Start the server (as a service), or using the command line manually by running the *lmadmin* file from the FlexNet server installation directory.

If you come across any issues while installing/running the software, please refer to[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Troubleshooting' space='IL2024x'].

## PAGE 00031: Installing FlexNet license server 11.12, 11.14, 11.16

- page_id: `136726262`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726262/Installing+FlexNet+license+server+11.12+11.14+11.16
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:21.217+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing > FlexNet license server 11.12, 11.14, 11.16
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### CONTENT-LAYER: For OS X and Linux users

1081226170

#### CONTENT-COLUMN: For OS X and Linux users

1081226182

1081226168

**On this page**

#### CONTENT-BLOCK: For OS X and Linux users

1081226172

#### EXCERPT: For OS X and Linux users

INLINE

##### Installation procedure

###### For Windows

1. Install the FlexNet license server manager. We highly recommend running the FlexNet license server (*lmadmin*) as a service (on Windows).As a result, the server can start automatically after the machine boots. Starting the server manually is not user-friendly – there is no GUI for this action.If your operating system is Windows, you only need to select the **Run as a service** check box when prompted during the *lmadmin* installation.[IMAGE alt='' src='']For the instructions on how to create a daemon, refer to Automatic Start in:[ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf'][ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf']
2. Place the vendor daemon - Cameo into the FlexNet server install folder. If you use *lmadmin*, do the following:
  1. Open the FlexNet server installation folder.
  2. In the open folder, create the licenses\cameo folder.
  3. Place the vendor daemon in *<FlexNet server installation folder>\licenses\cameo*. 
[IMAGE alt='' src=''] Note that all files in FNPLicenseServerManager must have read/write permissions. *lmadmin* or cameo daemon may not start even if a log file or cameo daemon does not have r/w permissions.Use this command to set permissions for all files within the directory recursively.chmod -R 755 FNPLicenseServerManager
3. Start the server by running the *lmadmin* file from the FlexNet server installation directory.

###### For Linux

1. Install the FlexNet license server manager. We highly recommend running the FlexNet license server (*lmadmin*) as a daemon (on OS X or Linux).As a result, the server can start automatically after the machine boots. Starting the server manually is not user-friendly – there is no GUI for this action.For the instructions on how to create a daemon, refer to Automatic Start in:[ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf'][ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf']
2. Place the vendor daemon - Cameo into the FlexNet server install folder. If you use *lmadmin*, do the following:
  1. Open the FlexNet server installation folder. For OS X and Linux usersIf you don't have permission to open the FlexNet server installation folder, execute the following command from the root:On OS X 
chmod g+x FNPLicenseServerManager/ 
chmod –R g+w ./*On Linuxchmod g+x FNPLicenseServerManager/
  2. In the open folder, create the licenses\cameo folder.
  3. Place the vendor daemon in *<FlexNet server installation folder>\licenses\cameo*.
3. Start the server by running the lmadmin file from the FlexNet server installation directory.

If you come across any issues while installing/running the software, please refer to[Troubleshooting](https://docs.nomagic.com/display/NMDOC/Troubleshooting).

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726192 space=IL2024x version=4 -->
## PAGE 00032: Installing modeling tools

- page_id: `136726192`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726192/Installing+modeling+tools
- version_number: 4
- version_date: `2024-05-15T15:22:22.264+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Installing modeling tools and plugins
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### CONTENT-LAYER: Note

391035911

INLINE

#### CONTENT-BLOCK: Note

#### EXCERPT: Note
