##### Prerequisites

- Ensure your machine meets the minimum [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='System requirements' space=''] for running the modeling tool.
- An appropriate [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Java version support' space='NMDOC'] should be installed on your machine (optional).
- **IMPORTANT for [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DSLS installation and licensing' space='ILTWRT']**. Microsoft Visual C++ Redistributable must be installed (see Latest supported Visual C++ Redistributable downloads ). This applies to Windows OS only.
- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space='']

##### Installation workflow

1. Install the modeling tool following the installation instructions according to your operating system. Demo Version filesStarting with19.0 SP2, Demo version comes as a separate install file anddoes not requirethe license key.
2. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space=''] the license key or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space='']the floating license.

#### WARNING: For the users of Academic license

For the users of Academic license

By default, the licensing information is stored in each user's home directory. If you are using the Academic license in class, we recommend saving the configuration files (which include the licensing information) in the modeling tool installation directory. The applied academic license will be available for all users of the particular machine when the configuration files are stored in the recommended location. See the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] for instructions on changing the modeling tool configuration file location.

You must install the desktop software on your computer to use the modeling tool.The installation procedures provided below are for the standard installation as well as the advanced. However, it is strongly recommended to use the standard installation procedure.

##### **Installing on Windows**

###### **Standard installation**

1. Double-click the installer.
2. If the User Account Control dialog appears asking permission for the installer to make changes in your computer, click Yes .
3. Follow the on-screen instructions.
4. Start the modeling tool by doing one of the following: ImportantWe recommend starting the modeling tool as an administrator. Right-click the *<modeling tool>.exe* file. Select **Run as administrator** from the shortcut menu.
  - On the taskbar in Windows, click the Start button, and then, click the modeling tool (for example, MagicDraw) .
  - Open the *<modeling tool> installation*\*bin* folder and double-click the modeling tool .exe file (for example, m*agicdraw.exe)*.
5. In the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] dialog, do one of the following:
  - If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click Import .
  - If you want to use the default environment options, click Use Default .
6. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space=''] the floating license.

###### Installation using no-installer

#### WARNING: Important

Important

This is an advanced procedure for installing the modeling tool. Please use this procedure only if you are familiar with the modeling tool and/or the standard installation does not support your use case.

#### NOTE: Note

Note

An appropriate[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Java version support' space='NMDOC']should be installed on your computer before you begin.

1. Extract <modeling tool>_<version number> _no_install.zip .
2. Set Java home:
  1. Open the <modeling tool>.properties file, which can be found in <modeling tool>_<version number> _no_install\bin folder.
  2. In the JAVA_HOME line, add the path to the Java software. For example: JAVA_HOME=C\:\\Program Files\\Java\\jdk11.0.9
3. To start the modeling tool, open the <modeling tool>_<version number> _ no_install\bin folder and double-click the <modeling tool>.exe file.
4. In the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] dialog, do one of the following:
  - If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click Import .
  - If you want to use the default environment options, click Use Default .
5. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space=''] the floating license.

##### **Installing on OS X**

###### **Standard installation**

1. Double-click the installer.
2. In the modeling tool installation window, drag the <modeling tool> folder to the Applications folder.
3. Close the modeling tool installation window.
4. Start the modeling tool. Open the Application / <modeling tool> installation folder and double-click the modeling tool .app file (for example, MagicDraw.app) .
5. In the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] dialog, do one of the following:
  - If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click Import .
  - If you want to use the default environment options, click Use Default .
6. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space=''] the floating license.

#### NOTE: Note

Note

If the message appears asking permission to open the file, click **Open**.

###### Installation using no-installer

#### WARNING: Important

Important

This is an advanced procedure for installing the modeling tool. Please use this procedure only if you are familiar with the modeling tool and/or the standard installation does not support your use case.

#### NOTE: Note

Note

An appropriate[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Java version support' space='NMDOC']should be installed on your computer before you begin.

1. Extract <modeling tool>_ <version number>_no_instal.zip .
2. Set Java home:
  1. Open the <modeling tool>.properties file, which can be found in <modeling tool>_<version number> _no_install\bin folder.
  2. In the JAVA_HOME line, add the path to the Java software. For example: JAVA_HOME= /Users/<user_name>/Library/Java/JavaVirtualMachines/jdk11.0.9.jdk/Contents/Home/
3. To start the modeling tool, open the <modeling tool>_<version number> _no_install folder and double-click the <modeling tool>.app file.
4. In the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] dialog, do one of the following:
  - If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click Import .
  - If you want to use the default environment options, click Use Default .
5. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space=''] the floating license.

##### **Installing on Unix**

###### **Standard installation**

1. From the <modeling tool>_ <version number>_unix.sh shortcut menu, select the Properties command and then click to select the Allow executing file as program check box.
2. Double-click the installer.
3. Follow the on-screen instructions to install the modeling tool.
4. Start the modeling tool. Open the <modeling tool> installation/bin folder and double-click the modeling tool file (for example, magicdraw).
5. In the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] dialog, do one of the following:
  - If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click Import .
  - If you want to use the default environment options, click Use Default .
6. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space=''] the floating license.

###### Installation using no-installer

#### WARNING: Important

Important

This is an advanced procedure for installing the modeling tool. Please use this procedure only if you are familiar with the modeling tool and/or the standard installation does not support your use case.

#### NOTE: Note

Note

An appropriate[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Java version support' space='NMDOC']should be installed on your computer before you begin.

1. Extract <modeling tool>_<version number> _no_install.zip .
2. Set Java home:
  1. Open the <modeling tool> .properties file, which can be found in <modeling tool>_<version number> _no_install\bin folder.
  2. In the JAVA_HOME line, add the path to the Java software. For example: JAVA_HOME=/usr/local/java/jre11.0.9
3. To start the modeling tool, open the <modeling tool>_<version number> _ no_install/bin folder and double-click the <modeling tool> file.
4. In the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Configuration files' space='MD2024x'] dialog, do one of the following:
  - If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click Import .
  - If you want to use the default environment options, click Use Default .
5. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space=''] the floating license.

##### Bundling JRE for multiple operating systems

If you want to configure the modeling tool for multiple operating systems, you can manually customize the *<modeling tool>.properties* file in order for the tool to automatically detect the relevant operating system upon its launch. This eliminates the need to customize the JRE path on each individual operating system where the bundled modeling tool is used.

JREs should be bundled for each operating system in different subdirectories.

1. Open the <modeling tool>.properties file, which can be found in <modeling tool>_<version number> _no_install\bin folder.
2. In the JAVA_HOME line, add the path to the Java software for a specific operating system. Duplicate the line for any additional operating systems you may be using, adding their relative paths. For example:

*JAVA_HOME_WINDOWS=jre/windows**JAVA_HOME_MACOSX=jre/macosx/mac/Contents/Home/jre**JAVA_HOME_LINUX=jre/linux*

When you are finished with the installation, the following page will provide you with more information onsetting up your modeling tool:

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing plugins' space='']

If you will be using a floating license server, all relevant information can be found here:

- [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server installation and licensing' space='']

If you run into further problems with installation, please try:

- checking the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Frequently Asked Questions' space='FAQ'] for known problems
- checking the [No Magic Community forum](https://community.nomagic.com/)
- or contacting customer [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Support_obsolete' space='NMDOC'].

However, it is strongly recommended to use the standard installation procedure</span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">.</span></p><h3 class="style1"><strong>Installing on Windows</strong></h3><h4><strong>Standard installation</strong></h4><ol><li>Double-click the installer.</li><li>If the <strong>User Account Control </strong>dialog appears asking permission for the installer to make changes in your computer, click <strong>Yes</strong>.</li><li>Follow the on-screen instructions.</li><li><p>Start the modeling tool by doing one of the following:</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="8baa0977-6720-4878-8851-2301b039700d"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Important</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p><span class="diffcontext">We recommend starting the modeling tool as an administrator. Right-click the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.exe</em> file. Select <strong>Run as administrator</strong> from the shortcut menu.</span></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ul><li>On the taskbar in Windows, click the <strong>Start</strong> button, and then, click the modeling tool (for example, <em>MagicDraw)</em>.</li><li><p>Open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt; installation</em>\<em>bin</em> folder and double-click the modeling tool .exe file (for example, m<em>agicdraw.exe)</em>.</p></li></ul></li><li><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);">In the </span><strong><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="MD2024x" ri:content-title="Configuration files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Import Configuration]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></strong><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);"> dialog, do one of the following:</span><ul class="style1"><li>If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click <strong>Import</strong>.</li><li>If you want to use the default environment options, click <strong>Use Default</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Adding the license key" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Add the license key]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> <span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">or </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[obtain ]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">the </span>floating<span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> license.</span></li></ol><p><br /></p><h4>Installation using no-installer</h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="warning" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="9abca5c7-3bc9-4b02-b929-8d9a845de5cc"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Important</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p>This is an advanced procedure for installing the modeling tool. Please use this procedure only if you are familiar with the modeling tool and/or the standard installation does not support your use case.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="d125575d-a244-4089-b6ed-be2f72272839"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Note</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">An appropriate </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="NMDOC" ri:content-title="Java version support" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[JVM version]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> should be installed on your computer before you begin.</span></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ol><li>Extract <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em><em>_no_install.zip</em>.</li><li>Set Java home:<ol><li>Open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.properties</em> file, which can be found in <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em><em>_no_install\bin</em> folder.</li><li>In the <em>JAVA_HOME</em> line, add the path to the Java software. For example:<br /><em><ac:inline-comment-marker ac:ref="6bb2f95d-3fae-4f9a-ab29-b1d681014b09">JAVA_HOME=C\:\\Program Files\\Java\\jdk11.0.9</ac:inline-comment-marker></em></li></ol></li><li>To start the modeling tool, open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em>_<em>no_install\bin</em> folder and double-click the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.exe</em> file.</li><li><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);">In the </span><strong><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="MD2024x" ri:content-title="Configuration files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Import Configuration]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></strong><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);"> dialog, do one of the following:</span><ul class="style1"><li>If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click <strong>Import</strong>.</li><li>If you want to use the default environment options, click <strong>Use Default</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Adding the license key" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Add the license key]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> </span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">or </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[obtain ]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">the </span><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">floating</span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> license.</span></li></ol><h3 class="style1"><strong>Installing on OS X</strong></h3><h4><strong>Standard installation</strong></h4><ol><li>Double-click the installer.</li><li>In the modeling tool installation window, drag the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;</em> folder to the <em>Applications</em> folder.</li><li>Close the <em>modeling tool</em> installation window.</li><li>Start the modeling tool. Open the <em>Application</em> / <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt; installation</em> folder and double-click the modeling tool .app file (for example, <em>MagicDraw.app)</em>.</li><li><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);">In the </span><strong><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="MD2024x" ri:content-title="Configuration files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Import Configuration]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></strong><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);"> dialog, do one of the following:</span><ul class="style1"><li>If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click <strong>Import</strong>.</li><li>If you want to use the default environment options, click <strong>Use Default</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Adding the license key" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Add the license key]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> </span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">or </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[obtain ]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">the </span><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">floating</span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> license.</span><p><br /></p></li></ol><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="01c10d62-195c-4d03-b6f5-8b0b4540773d"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Note</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p>If the message appears asking permission to open the file, click <strong>Open</strong>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><h4>Installation using no-installer</h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="warning" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="2a342638-bd1d-4bc6-90c2-5eb53b8007f2"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Important</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p>This is an advanced procedure for installing the modeling tool. Please use this procedure only if you are familiar with the modeling tool and/or the standard installation does not support your use case.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="1211027b-d81e-4a2a-88ec-a745ef3c5687"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Note</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">An appropriate </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="NMDOC" ri:content-title="Java version support" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[JVM version]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> should be installed on your computer before you begin.</span></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ol><li>Extract <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_</em><em>&lt;version number&gt;_no_instal.zip</em>.</li><li>Set Java home:<ol><li>Open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.properties</em> file, which can be found in <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em><em>_no_install\bin</em> folder.</li><li>In the <em>JAVA_HOME</em> line, add the path to the Java software. For example:<br />JAVA_HOME=<em>/Users/&lt;user_name&gt;/Library/Java/JavaVirtualMachines/jdk11.0.9.jdk/Contents/Home/</em></li></ol></li><li>To start the modeling tool, open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em><em>_no_install</em> folder and double-click the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.app</em> file.</li><li><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);">In the </span><strong><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="MD2024x" ri:content-title="Configuration files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Import Configuration]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></strong><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);"> dialog, do one of the following:</span><ul class="style1"><li>If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click <strong>Import</strong>.</li><li>If you want to use the default environment options, click <strong>Use Default</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Adding the license key" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Add the license key]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> </span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">or </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[obtain ]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">the </span><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">floating</span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> license.</span></li></ol><h3><strong>Installing on Unix</strong></h3><h4><strong>Standard installation</strong></h4><ol><li>From the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_</em><em>&lt;version number&gt;_unix.sh</em> shortcut menu, select the <strong>Properties</strong> command and then click to select the <strong>Allow executing file as program</strong> check box. </li><li>Double-click the installer.</li><li>Follow the on-screen instructions to install the modeling tool.</li><li>Start the modeling tool. Open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt; installation/bin</em> folder and double-click the modeling tool file (for example, <em>magicdraw).</em></li><li><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);">In the </span><strong><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="MD2024x" ri:content-title="Configuration files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Import Configuration]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></strong><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);"> dialog, do one of the following:</span><ul class="style1"><li>If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click <strong>Import</strong>.</li><li>If you want to use the default environment options, click <strong>Use Default</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Adding the license key" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Add the license key]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> </span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">or </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[obtain ]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">the </span><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">floating</span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> license.</span><p><br /></p></li></ol><h4>Installation using no-installer</h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="warning" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="aca76ddc-488c-445e-a1a3-408ed68259f5"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Important</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p>This is an advanced procedure for installing the modeling tool. Please use this procedure only if you are familiar with the modeling tool and/or the standard installation does not support your use case.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="7e3974a9-965c-426e-9e97-d8e4779e066c"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Note</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">An appropriate </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="NMDOC" ri:content-title="Java version support" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[JVM version]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> should be installed on your computer before you begin.</span></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ol><li>Extract <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em><em>_no_install.zip</em>.</li><li>Set Java home:<ol><li>Open the &lt;modeling tool&gt;<em>.properties</em> file, which can be found in <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em><em>_no_install\bin</em> folder.</li><li>In the <em>JAVA_HOME</em> line, add the path to the Java software. For example:<br /><em>JAVA_HOME=/usr/local/java/jre11.0.9</em></li></ol></li><li>To start the modeling tool, open the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em>_<em>no_install/bin </em>folder and double-click the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;</em> file.</li><li><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);">In the </span><strong><ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="MD2024x" ri:content-title="Configuration files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Import Configuration]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></strong><span style="color: rgb(24,24,24);"> dialog, do one of the following:</span><ul class="style1"><li>If you want to import the environment options from an earlier modeling tool version, select the location and click <strong>Import</strong>.</li><li>If you want to use the default environment options, click <strong>Use Default</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Adding the license key" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[Add the license key]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> </span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">or </span><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[obtain ]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);">the </span><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">floating</span><span style="color: rgb(68,68,68);"> license.</span></li></ol><h3>Bundling JRE for multiple operating systems</h3><p>If you want to configure the modeling tool for multiple operating systems, you can manually customize the <em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.properties</em> file in order for the tool to automatically detect the relevant operating system upon its launch. This eliminates the need to customize the JRE path on each individual operating system where the bundled modeling tool is used. </p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="5d9c320a-ea52-4e80-93db-c0d1cf64c43b"><ac:rich-text-body><p>JREs should be bundled for each operating system in different subdirectories.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ol><li><span>Open the </span><em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;.properties</em><span> file, which can be found in </span><em>&lt;modeling tool&gt;_&lt;version number&gt;</em><em>_no_install\bin</em><span> folder.</span></li><li><span>In the </span><em>JAVA_HOME</em><span> line, add the path to the Java software for a specific operating system. Duplicate the line for any additional operating systems you may be using, adding their relative paths. For example:</span></li></ol><p style="margin-left: 60.0px;"><em>JAVA_HOME_WINDOWS=jre/windows<br /></em><em>JAVA_HOME_MACOSX=jre/macosx/mac/Contents/Home/jre<br /></em><em>JAVA_HOME_LINUX=jre/linux</em></p><p><br /></p><p><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">When you are finished with the installation, the following page will provide you with more information on </span><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">setting up your modeling tool:</span></p><ul><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Installing plugins" /></ac:link></li></ul><p>If you will be using a floating license server, all relevant information can be found here:</p><ul><li><ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="FlexNet license server installation and licensing" /></ac:link></li></ul><p><br /></p><p><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">If you run into further problems with installation, please try:</span></p><ul><li><span style="color: rgb(255,0,0);"><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">checking the</span> <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="FAQ" ri:content-title="Frequently Asked Questions" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[FAQ section]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">for known problems</span></span></li><li><span style="color: rgb(255,0,0);"><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">checking the</span> <a href="https://community.nomagic.com/">No Magic Community forum</a></span></li><li><span style="color: rgb(255,0,0);"><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">or contacting customer <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Support_obsolete" ri:space-key="NMDOC" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[support]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link>.</span></span></li></ul></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p>
````

## PAGE 00033: Installing modeling tools and plugins

- page_id: `136726191`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726191/Installing+modeling+tools+and+plugins
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:17.902+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

INLINE

The section explains how to perform the standard step-by-step installation and no-install run of Magic Software Architect, Magic Cyber Systems Engineer, Magic Systems of Systems Architect, MagicDraw, Cameo Systems Modeler, and Cameo Enterprise Architecture modeling tools on Windows, OSx, and Unix. Additionally, it focuses on the installation of plugins in modeling tools. You will learn how to install a plugin from the downloaded .zip archive and install a plugin manually.

Additionally, it focuses on the installation of plugins in modeling tools. You will learn how to install a plugin from the downloaded .zip archive and install a plugin manually. </span></p><p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="children" ac:schema-version="2" ac:macro-id="b30777df-69af-4603-9e70-34b304466351" /></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p>

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726193 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00034: Installing plugins

- page_id: `136726193`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726193/Installing+plugins
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:18.340+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Installing modeling tools and plugins
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

For information about plugin installation in versions prior to the 2022x version, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing plugins in earlier versions' space=''] page.

#### EXCERPT: Getting help

INLINE

Choose one of the following ways to install a plugin in a modeling tool:

- 
- 
  - Adding plugins from an *.rdzip* file located on a local file system or network share
  - 
- 
  - Installing an individual plugin by importing a *.zip* file
  - Installing an individual plugin by extracting a *.zip* file

##### Installing our commercial and no-cost plugins

All available plugins provided by us, both commercial and no-cost, are accessible via the *core.rdzip* file, which is pre-bundled together with the installation files and is readily available in the **Resource/Plugin Manager**. The available plugins depend on the modeling tool that you are using. The file is located at *<tool_installation_directory>\data\resourcemanager\distribution\core.rdzip*, however, it is added automatically to the **Resource/Plugin Manager**.

Add pre-bundled plugin bundleTo install our commercial and no-cost plugins

1. In the main menu, select Help > Resource/Plugin Manager . The pre-bundled core.rdzip file containing all available plugins is loaded automatically.
2. Select the check boxes for the plugins you want to install.
3. Click the **Download/Install**button to install the selected plugins.
4. Restart your modeling tool. 
[IMAGE alt='' src='']

##### Install custom pluginsInstalling custom plugins

If you are using custom-built plugin *.rdzip* files located on a local file system, network share, or a web server, you can add the plugins from the file by specifying its location via the **Resource/Plugin Manager**.

###### Adding plugins from a local file system or network shareAdding plugins from an *.rdzip* file located on a local file system or network share

To add plugins from an*.rdzip* file located on a local file system or network share

1. In the main menu, select Help > Resource/Plugin Manager .
2. In the Resource Location section, click the [ATTACHMENT filename='three_dot_button.png'] button.
3. In the **Manage Resource Locations** dialog, click **Add**. 
[IMAGE alt='' src=''] You can manage the list displayed in the **Manage Resource Locations** dialog by adding, removing, or reordering the resource locations.
4. The Select Resource Location or Distribution File dialog opens. Specify the location of the plugin bundle ( .rdzip ) file and click Open . The resource location is added.
5. Click **OK**to import the resources.
6. Select the check boxes for the plugins you want to install.
7. Click the **Download/Install**button to install the selected plugins.
8. Restart your modeling tool. You can extract an *.rdzip* file and then . [IMAGE alt='' src='']

###### Adding plugins from a web serverAdding plugins from a web server

You can also obtain the needed plugins from a web server if you do not have the .*rdzip* file but have been provided a URL by your license manager.

Installing plugins from a web serverTo add plugins from a web server

1. In the main menu, select Help > Resource/Plugin Manager .
2. In the Resource Location section, click the [ATTACHMENT filename='three_dot_button.png'] button.
3. In the Manage Resource Locations dialog, click Add URL . The Resource Server URL dialog opens.
4. In the Resource Server URL dialog, type or paste the server address. [ATTACHMENT filename='adding_resource_server_url.png']
5. Click OK . The plugins from the selected location are listed in the Resource/Plugin Manager .

##### Other plugin installation optionsOther plugin installation options

The default and the recommended option is to use the pre-bundled *core.rdzip* file which is added automatically, however, you can also install individual plugins from their *.zip* files.

###### Installing an individual plugin by importing a *.zip*file

Installing an individual plugin by importing a .zip fileTo install an individual plugin by importing a *.zip*file

1. In the main menu, select Help > Resource/Plugin Manager .
2. Click the Import button and specify the location of the archived plugin file ( .zip ) and click Open . The plugin is extracted and installed automatically.
3. Restart your modeling tool. The **Import** button is used to install only an individual plugin by importing an archived plugin file (*.zip*). To install plugins from an *.rdzip* plugin bundle file, you need to add the *.rdzip* file by specifying its **Resource Location**. [IMAGE alt='' src='']

###### Installing an individual plugin by extracting a *.zip* file

Installing an individual plugin by extracting a .zip fileTo install an individual plugin by extracting a .*zip* file

1. Extract an archived plugin file ( .zip ) file to the same directory where your modeling tool is installed.
2. Start the modeling tool. The plugin is installed on your modeling tool.

#### TIP: Getting help

Getting help

If you run into any installation-related problems, try the following:

- Check the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Frequently Asked Questions' space='FAQ'] for known problems.
- Check the [No Magic Community forum.](https://community.nomagic.com/)
- Contact [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Support_obsolete' space='NMDOC'].

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

is readily available in the <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>. The available plugins depend on the modeling tool that you are using. The file is located at <em>&lt;tool_installation_directory&gt;\data\resourcemanager\distribution\core.rdzip</em>, however, it is added automatically to the <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>.</p><p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="befc40f1-9f40-4872-a6ea-254e203acb2b"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Add pre-bundled plugin bundle</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>To install our commercial and no-cost plugins</p><hr /><ol><li>In the main menu, select <strong>Help</strong> &gt; <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>. The pre-bundled <em>core.rdzip</em> file containing all available plugins is loaded automatically.</li><li>Select the check boxes for the plugins you want to install.</li><li><p class="auto-cursor-target _mce_tagged_br">Click the <strong>Download/Install </strong>button to install the selected plugins.</p></li><li><p class="auto-cursor-target">Restart your modeling tool.<br /><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="Install_a_plugin_through_the_pre-bundled_plugin_file.png" /></ac:image></p></li></ol><h3><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="2382a198-ede7-45b0-9d2f-ee3ae9cb9f79"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Install custom plugins</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>Installing custom plugins</h3><p>If you are using custom-built plugin <em>.rdzip</em> files located on a local file system, network share, or a web server, you can add the plugins from the file by specifying its location via the <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>.</p><h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="1ed2e0fa-0b78-464c-b125-03703c19c347"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Adding plugins from a local file system or network share</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>Adding plugins from an <em>.rdzip</em> file located on a local file system or network share</h4><p>To add plugins from an<em> .rdzip</em> file located on a local file system or network share</p><hr /><ol><li>In the main menu, select <strong>Help</strong> &gt; <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>.</li><li>In the <strong>Resource Location</strong> section, click the <ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="three_dot_button.png" /></ac:image> button.</li><li><p class="auto-cursor-target">In the <strong>Manage Resource Locations</strong> dialog, click <strong>Add</strong>.<br /><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="manage_resource_locations_dialog.png" /></ac:image></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="e487dbde-2d43-4af6-87b0-d386bdceeb13"><ac:rich-text-body><p>You can manage the list displayed in the <strong>Manage Resource Locations</strong> dialog by adding, removing, or reordering the resource locations.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></li><li>The <strong>Select Resource Location or Distribution File</strong> dialog opens. Specify the location of the plugin bundle (<em>.rdzip</em>) file and click<strong> Open</strong>. The resource location is added.</li><li><p class="auto-cursor-target _mce_tagged_br">Click <strong>OK </strong>to import the resources.</p></li><li>Select the check boxes for the plugins you want to install. </li><li><p class="auto-cursor-target _mce_tagged_br">Click the <strong>Download/Install </strong>button to install the selected plugins.</p></li><li><p class="auto-cursor-target">Restart your modeling tool.</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="5e58112d-1502-43f2-ad1b-0de0c7a2e82a"><ac:rich-text-body><p>You can extract an <em>.rdzip</em> file and then <ac:link ac:anchor="Installing an individual plugin by importing a .zip file"><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[add selected plugins individually]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="Installing_a_plugin_by_adding_a_plugin_bundle.png" /></ac:image></p></li></ol><h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="1a446d22-3ea3-46a8-ad8e-ee20ab6ee5e8"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Adding plugins from a web server</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>Adding plugins from a web server</h4><p>You can also obtain the needed plugins from a web server if you do not have the .<em>rdzip</em> file but have been provided a URL by your license manager.</p><p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="587cacf4-c529-411d-bbff-27e867399129"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Installing plugins from a web server </ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>To add plugins from a web server</p><hr /><ol><li>In the main menu, select <strong>Help</strong> &gt; <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>.</li><li>In the <strong>Resource Location</strong> section, click the <ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="three_dot_button.png" /></ac:image> button.</li><li>In the <strong>Manage Resource Locations</strong> dialog, click <strong>Add URL</strong>. The <strong>Resource Server URL</strong> dialog opens.</li><li>In the <strong>Resource Server URL</strong> dialog, type or paste the server address.<br /><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="adding_resource_server_url.png" /></ac:image></li><li>Click <strong>OK</strong>. The plugins from the selected location are listed in the <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>.</li></ol><h3><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="7544c9c5-c555-4923-8cb4-56b406f84321"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Other plugin installation options</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>Other plugin installation options</h3><p>The default and the recommended option is to <ac:link ac:anchor="Add pre-bundled plugin bundle"><ac:link-body>use the pre-bundled <em>core.rdzip</em> file</ac:link-body></ac:link> which is added automatically, however, you can also install individual plugins from their <em>.zip</em> files.</p><h4>Installing an individual plugin by importing a <em>.zip </em>file </h4><p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="4fb9169c-08e1-4b4a-a62a-84d4b1e068da"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Installing an individual plugin by importing a .zip file </ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>To install an individual plugin by importing a <em>.zip </em>file </p><hr /><ol><li>In the main menu, select <strong>Help</strong> &gt; <strong>Resource/Plugin Manager</strong>.</li><li>Click the <strong>Import</strong> button and specify the location of the archived plugin file (<em>.zip</em>) and click <strong>Open</strong>. The plugin is extracted and installed automatically.</li><li><p class="auto-cursor-target">Restart your modeling tool.</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="note" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="f179563d-593b-43e4-a9f7-1ed3980b26ac"><ac:rich-text-body><p>The <strong>Import</strong> button is used to install only an individual plugin by importing an archived plugin file (<em>.zip</em>). To install plugins from an <em>.rdzip</em> plugin bundle file, you need to add the <em>.rdzip</em> file by <ac:link ac:anchor="Adding plugins from a local file system or network share"><ac:link-body>specifying its <strong>Resource Location</strong></ac:link-body></ac:link>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><ac:image><ri:attachment ri:filename="Installing_an_individual_plugin.png" /></ac:image></p></li></ol><h4>Installing an individual plugin by extracting a <em>.zip</em> file</h4><p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="anchor" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="723543ef-93f9-4cba-82d4-3330fe44ab16"><ac:parameter ac:name="">Installing an individual plugin by extracting a .zip file</ac:parameter></ac:structured-macro>To install an individual plugin by extracting a .<em>zip</em> file</p><hr /><ol><li>Extract an archived plugin file (<em>.zip</em>) file to the same directory where your modeling tool is installed.</li><li>Start the modeling tool. The plugin is installed on your modeling tool.</li></ol><p><br /></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="tip" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="38679957-e001-4681-bd27-eb87f42edcce"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">Getting help</ac:parameter><ac:rich-text-body><p><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">If you run into any installation-related problems, try the following:</span></p><ul><li><span style="color: rgb(255,0,0);"><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">Check the</span> <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="FAQ" ri:content-title="Frequently Asked Questions" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[FAQ section]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> <span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">for known problems.</span></span></li><li><span style="color: rgb(255,0,0);"><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">Check the</span> <a href="https://community.nomagic.com/" class="external-link" rel="nofollow">No Magic Community forum<span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">.</span></a></span></li><li><span style="color: rgb(255,0,0);"><span style="color: rgb(0,0,0);">Contact <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Support_obsolete" ri:space-key="NMDOC" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[customer support]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link>.</span></span></li></ul></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p>

## PAGE 00035: Installing plugins in earlier versions

- page_id: `136726200`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726200/Installing+plugins+in+earlier+versions
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:18.651+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Installing modeling tools and plugins > Installing plugins
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### CONTENT-LAYER: Getting help

391665676

#### CONTENT-COLUMN: Getting help

391665680

#### CONTENT-BLOCK: Getting help

391665678

For information about plugin installation in 2022x version and later, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing plugins' space=''] page.

#### EXCERPT: Getting help

INLINE

Choose one of the following ways to install a plugin in a modeling tool:

- Install a plugin bundle (.rdzip) via the **Resource/Plugin Manager** dialog. For information on how to download the plugin bundle, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space=''].
- Install an individually purchased archived plugin file (.zip) via the **Resource/Plugin Manager** dialog.
- .
- .

To install a plugin bundle (.rdzip) via the Resource/Plugin Manager dialog To install a plugin bundle (.rdzip) via the **Resource/Plugin Manager** dialog

1. Start your modeling tool.
2. From the modeling tool main menu, select Help > Resource/Plugin Manager .
3. Click the [ATTACHMENT filename='three_dot_button.png'] button.
4. In the Manage Resource Locations dialog, click Add . The Select Resource Location or Distribution File dialog opens.
5. Specify the location of a plugin bundle (.rdzip) file and click Open . The resource location is added.
6. Click **OK**to import resources.

You can extract the .rdzip file and then .

adding individual pluginsTo install an individual plugin from an archive file (.zip) via the **Resource/Plugin Manager** dialog

1. Start your modeling tool.
2. From the main menu of a modeling tool, select Help > Resource/Plugin Manager .
3. Click the Import button and specify the location of an archived plugin file (.zip) and click Open . The plugin is extracted and installed automatically.
4. Restart your modeling tool.

Install a plugin manually To install a plugin manually

1. Extract an archived plugin file (.zip) file to the same directory where your modeling tool is installed.
2. Start the modeling tool. The plugin is applied to your modeling tool.

You can also obtain the needed resources from a web server if you do not have the .*rdzip* file but have been provided with an URL by your license manager.

Obtain and install a plugin from a web server To specify the server where the resources and their descriptor file are located

1. Open Resource/Plugin Manager and click [ATTACHMENT filename='three_dot_button.png'] .
2. In the Manage Resource Locations dialog, click Add URL . The Resource Server URL dialog opens.
3. In the open Resource Server URL dialog, type or paste the server address. [ATTACHMENT filename='adding_resource_server_url.png']
4. Click OK .

The resources from the selected location are listed in the **Resource/Plugin Manager**.

#### TIP: Getting help

Getting help

If you run into any installation-related problems, try the following:

- Check the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Frequently Asked Questions' space='FAQ'] for known problems.
- Check the [No Magic Community forum](https://community.nomagic.com/).
- Contact [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Support_obsolete' space='NMDOC'].

## PAGE 00037: Java version support for 19.0 SP2

- page_id: `249579959`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/249579959/Java+version+support+for+19.0+SP2
- version_number: 2
- version_date: `2025-09-02T14:08:04.048+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Java version support
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### INFO: Changing JVM version

Changing JVM version

For the information on how to change the JVM version, please see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='How to change JVM version' space='']

Starting with 19.0 SP2, all the modeling tools, plugins, and collaboration tools were tested with OpenJDK* as an alternative to Oracle JDK.

In the following table, please find the recommendations for the appropriate Java version.

| Product | Version | Recommended | Alternative | Included into installation files |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| MagicDrawCameo Systems ModelerCameo Enterprise ArchitectureMagic Software ArchitectMagic Cyber Systems EngineerMagic Systems of Systems Architect | 19.0 SP2 | Oracle JDK 8Windows, Linux: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_202Mac: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_102 | OpenJDK 8(1.8.0_192) | Oracle JDK 8Windows: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_202Mac: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_102 |
| Teamwork CloudTeamwork Server | 19.0 SP2 | Oracle JDK 8Windows, Linux: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_202Mac: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_102 | OpenJDK 8(1.8.0_192) | Oracle JDK 8Windows: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_202Mac: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_102 |
| Cameo Collaborator for Teamwork CloudWeb Application PlatformResourcesTWCloud Admin Console NG | 19.0 SP2 | OpenJDK 11 (2018-09-25 update) | Oracle JDK 11 | OpenJDK 11 (2018-09-25 update) |

For the information on how to change the JVM version, please see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='How to change JVM version' space='']

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| MagicDrawCameo Systems ModelerCameo Enterprise ArchitectureMagic Software ArchitectMagic Cyber Systems EngineerMagic Systems of Systems Architect | 19.0 SP3 | Oracle JDK 8Windows, Linux: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_202Mac: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_102 | OpenJDK 8(1.8.0_222) | Oracle JDK 8Windows: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_202Mac: Oracle JDK 1.8.0_102 |

- labels: []

#### INFO: Changing JVM version

Changing JVM version

For information on how to change the JVM version, please see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='How to change JVM version' space='']

In the following table, please find the recommendations for the appropriate Java version for 2021x.

| Product | Version | Recommended and included in installation files** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| MagicDrawCameo Systems ModelerCameo Enterprise ArchitectureMagic Software ArchitectMagic Cyber Systems EngineerMagic Systems of Systems Architect | 2021x | OpenJDK 11.0.9* (for all OS) |
| Teamwork Cloud | 2021x | OpenJDK 11.0.9* Cassandra 3.11.x requires JDK 8 (either Oracle or Open JDK). |
| Cameo Collaborator for Teamwork CloudWeb Application PlatformResourcesTWCloud Admin Console NG | 2021x | OpenJDK 14.0.1* |

***OpenJDK**. Based on the testing results, we recommend using OpenJDK HotSpot by AdoptJdk.

We strongly advise using the HotSpot distribution rather than OpenJ9. For more information, see "Help Me Choose" tips at [https://adoptopenjdk.net/](https://adoptopenjdk.net/).

**Java is included only in installation files for Windows and macOS. Linux installation files do not have built-in Java.

See the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='JVM recommendations for versions up to 19.0 SP1' space=''].

## PAGE 00042: Java version support for 2021x Refresh2

- page_id: `249579954`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/249579954/Java+version+support+for+2021x+Refresh2
- version_number: 2
- version_date: `2025-09-02T14:08:03.928+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Java version support
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### INFO: Changing JVM version

Changing JVM version

For information on how to change the JVM version, please see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='How to change JVM version' space='']

In the following table, please find the recommendations for the appropriate Java version for 2021x Refresh 2.

| Product | Version | Recommended and included in installation files** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| MagicDrawCameo Systems ModelerCameo Enterprise ArchitectureMagic Software ArchitectMagic Cyber Systems EngineerMagic Systems of Systems Architect | 2021x Refresh2 | OpenJDK 11.0.12* (for all OS) |
| Teamwork Cloud | 2021x Refresh2 | OpenJDK 11.0.12* Cassandra 3.11.x requires JDK 8 (either Oracle or Open JDK). |
| Cameo Collaborator for Teamwork CloudWeb Application PlatformResourcesTWCloud Admin Console NG | 2021x Refresh2 | OpenJDK 16.0.1* |

***OpenJDK**. Based on the testing results, we recommend using OpenJDK HotSpot by AdoptJdk.

OpenJ9 should not be used; instead, the HotSpot distribution should be utilized. For more information, see "Help Me Choose" tips at [https://adoptopenjdk.net/](https://adoptopenjdk.net/).

**Java is included only in installation files for Windows and macOS. Linux installation files do not have built-in Java.

See the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='JVM recommendations for versions up to 19.0 SP1' space=''].

For more information, see &quot;Help Me Choose&quot; tips at <a href="https://adoptopenjdk.net/">https://adoptopenjdk.net/</a>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p>**Java is included only in installation files for Windows and macOS. Linux installation files do not have built-in Java.</p><p>*** You should choose Java native to the macOS architecture (ARM or x86) in use.</p><hr /><p>See the <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="JVM recommendations for versions up to 19.0 SP1" /></ac:link>.</p><p>See <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="FAQ" ri:content-title="Zip exceptions thrown after Java version upgrade to 11.0.20+ or 17.0.8+" /></ac:link>.</p><p><br /></p><p style="text-align: center;"><br /></p>

## PAGE 00047: JVM recommendations for versions up to 19.0 SP1

- page_id: `249579960`

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**MagicDraw** and **Cameo Suite** products are Java based. 
The following table lists the **recommended* Java versions.**

* Most of testing was performed with these versions

****

**Please note, Oracle Java SE9 is not supported*.***

## PAGE 00048: License Manager

- page_id: `136726211`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726211/License+Manager
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:19.034+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Modeling tools and plugins licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

There are two ways to view the **License Manager** dialog:

- Starting the modeling tool for the very first time.
- Opening the dialog from the modeling tool's Help menu.

When you start the modeling tool for the first time, you will see the following dialog:

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

###### The License Manager dialog

In this dialog, you can select one of the license addition options according to the license you have.

| Button name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Use Floating License | If you have the credentials for a Floating license server, click to . |
| Select License Key File | If you have a seat, mobile, or academic license, click to . |
| Use in Reader Mode | To open the modeling tool in Reader Mode to read projects, click to . |
| Show Target ID | of your machine to be able to tie it with the license. |

When you need to change the license key file or obtain a floating license, you can open the**License Manager** dialog from the modeling tool menu (**Help** > **License Manager**).

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726184 space=IL2024x version=2 -->
## PAGE 00049: Managed licensing

- page_id: `136726184`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726184/Managed+licensing
- version_number: 2
- version_date: `2023-11-16T09:35:17.521+01:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Sales and licenses
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

DSLS (Dassault Systèmes License Server) is a licensing system developed by Dassault Systèmes that, in addition to seat and floating, also provides a managed licensing option.

Managed DSLS is also known as Managed Licensing Service.

With Managed DSLS, an on-premise customer no longer needs a physical machine to install DS License Server (DSLS). The license server is managed by Dassault Systèmes and located in the Dassault Systèmes Cloud datacenter.

Client machines authorized by the customer (authentication file) and located on the customer’s premises access the DSLS remotely. An administrator on the customer’s premises access the DSLS through a web interface using a login and a password.

For more information, please consult:

- *“Using The Managed Licensing Service” in the* DSLS Installation and Configuration Guide
- Managed DSLS Eligibility
- Managed DSLS maintenance

**Please contact your Dassault Systèmes sales representative in case you have an interest in Managed DSLS service.**

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<p><span style="color: rgb(62,63,64);">DSLS (Dassault Systèmes License Server) is a licensing system developed by Dassault Systèmes that, in addition to s</span>eat and floating, also <span style="color: rgb(62,63,64);">provides a</span> managed licensing option.</p><p class="bodytext" style="text-align: left;">Managed DSLS is also known as Managed Licensing Service.</p><p class="bodytext" style="text-align: left;">With Managed DSLS, an on-premise customer no longer needs a physical machine to install DS License Server (DSLS). The license server is managed by Dassault Systèmes and located in the Dassault Systèmes Cloud datacenter.</p><p class="bodytext" style="text-align: left;">Client machines authorized by the customer (authentication file) and located on the customer’s premises access the DSLS remotely. An administrator on the customer’s premises access the DSLS through a web interface using a login and a password.</p><p class="bodytext" style="text-align: left;">For more information, please consult:</p><ul style="text-align: left;"><li><strong><em>“Using The Managed Licensing Service” in the<span> </span></em></strong><a href="http://media.3ds.com/support/documentation/product/DS_License_Server/R2024x/DSLS-installation-and-configuration-guide.pdf?_gl=1*168vkyh*_ga*MjA1MDE4MDI3LjE2NjkwMTM5OTY.*_ga_DYJDKXYEZ4*MTcwMDEyMzUxMS40OS4wLjE3MDAxMjM1MTEuNjAuMC4w">DSLS Installation and Configuration Guide</a></li><li><a href="https://www.3ds.com/support/3dexperience-platform-on-cloud-support/eligibility/managed-dsls-eligibility/" style="text-decoration: none;" title="Opens internal link in current window">Managed DSLS Eligibility</a></li><li><a style="text-decoration: none;" title="Opens external link in new window" href="https://www.3ds.com/support/news/?woc=%7B%22support%20category%22%3A%5B%22support%20category%2Fmanaged%20dsls%20maintenance%22%5D%7D">Managed DSLS maintenance</a></li></ul><p class="bodytext" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Please contact your Dassault Systèmes sales representative in case you have an interest in Managed DSLS service.</strong></p>

## PAGE 00050: Modeling tools and plugins licensing

- page_id: `136726203`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726203/Modeling+tools+and+plugins+licensing
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:18.777+02:00`

- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

392027204

392027207

1243193542

**On this page**

4

392027205

The product license is identified by the license key. These are the types of license keys:

- FlexNet:
  - Seat
  - Floating
- DSLS:
  - Nodelock
  - Floating
  - Managed

Additionally, special licenses for the academic community are available: [https://www.nomagic.com/services/academic-research](https://www.nomagic.com/services/academic-research).

[IMAGE alt='' src='']

###### Licensing scheme

##### Licensing workflow

###### FlexNet Seat / DSLS Nodelock license

1. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Target ID' space='IL2024x'] .
2. Provide it to your sales representative.
3. Get a license key.
4. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding the license key' space='IL2024x']

###### Floating license

**FlexNet server license**

1. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Host ID or Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed' space='IL2024x'] [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Host ID or Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed' space='IL2024x']
2. Provide it to your sales representative.
3. Get a floating license key and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding a license to the FlexNet server' space='IL2024x']. Typically, this step is performed by the license server administrator.
4. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space='IL2024x']

**DSLS server license**

1. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining License Keys' space='IL2024x'] .
2. Provide it to your sales representative.
3. Get a floating license key and add it to the floating license server.
4. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool' space='IL2024x']

###### Managed license

Contact your Dassault Systèmes sales representative if you have an interest in Managed DSLS service. For more information, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Managed licensing' space='IL2024x'] page.

For more information, see the <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="IL2024x" ri:content-title="Managed licensing" /></ac:link> page.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro>
````

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726281 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00051: Modeling tools bundle

- page_id: `136726281`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726281/Modeling+tools+bundle
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:22.804+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**Creating a modeling tools bundle (Windows OS)**

Here, you can find the instructions on how to create a modeling tools bundle together with already installed plugins and defined options. A modeling tools bundle can be created by the Administrator or any responsible person and then provided to the company’s employees.

###### Advantages of using the modeling tools bundle

- Employees will receive the modeling tools bundle with already installed plugins - they will not need to spend time searching and installing required plugins.
- Employees will have the modeling tools bundle with already predefined [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Customizing environment options' space='MD2024x'] .

###### The most important environment options usually are

- Security certificates to enable secure communication between a modeling tool and Teamwork Cloud. See the bottom of the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Enabling secure connection between client and server' space='TWCloud2024x'] page.
- Floating License Server information
- Teamwork Cloud Server information
- Cameo Collaborator Server information

###### The modeling tools bundle can be prepared in the following way

1. The administrator installs a modeling tool on their computer.
2. The administrator installs all the required plugins and defines the options.
3. The administrator compresses the modeling tool installation folder.
4. The administrator extracts the modeling tools bundle on employee machines.

The employees need to start the modeling tool, and if they are using a seat license, they will need to apply and activate the license (or apply the already activated license provided for their machine).

For detailed steps, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Creating modeling tools bundle' space='IL2024x'] and [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Using modeling tools bundle' space='IL2024x'] pages.

###### Installation directories

By default, when you install a modeling tool, it writes to two separate directories:

1. Installation directory – C:\Program Files\<modeling tool name> (default).
2. Configuration directory – C:\Users\<your username>\AppData\Local\.<modeling_tool>\<version number>

###### Configuration files

The configuration files' locations are in folders named corresponding to the modeling tool name, e.g., */.cameo.systems.modeler/*for Cameo Systems Modeler and */cameoea/*for Cameo Enterprise Architecture. 
The properties files' names in the *bin* directory are also named *csm.properties* and *cameoea.properties,* corresponding to the product names.

###### Licensing

- Floating License . This works best for a pre-built bundle as the bundle can be configured with the license server information as part of the bundle. If your company uses floating licenses, the individuals will not have to use an individual seat license.
- Seat License .

For more information regarding available licensing options, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Modeling tools and plugins licensing' space='IL2024x'] page.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726241 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00052: Moving nodelocked modeling tool to another machine

- page_id: `136726241`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726241/Moving+nodelocked+modeling+tool+to+another+machine
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:20.154+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

INLINE

To move the nodelocked (locked to the particular machine) license from one machine to another:

1. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing modeling tools' space='IL2024x'] the modeling tool on a new machine.
2. Request a license key for a new machine (determine the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Target ID' space='IL2024x'] and provide it to your sales representative).
3. Get a new license key.
4. Start the modeling tool and add a license key.

Please note that you do not need to request for a new license key if you use a floating/shareable license.

movingTo move the FlexNet license server to another machine

2. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing FlexNet 11.17.0, 11.18.2, 11.19.0' space='IL2024x'] server version on the machine.
3. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding a license to the FlexNet server' space='IL2024x'] to the FlexNet server.

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726222 space=IL2024x version=3 -->
## PAGE 00054: Obtaining a floating license for a modeling tool

- page_id: `136726222`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726222/Obtaining+a+floating+license+for+a+modeling+tool
- version_number: 3
- version_date: `2024-10-16T16:14:04.931+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Modeling tools and plugins licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

**On this page**

5

##### Prerequisites

- The floating license server ( [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server installation and licensing' space=''] or [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DSLS installation and licensing' space=''] ) is installed and started.
- You have the floating license server name and port (provided by your system or license server administrator).

##### Procedure

1. Start the modeling tool.
2. When the **License Manager** dialog opens, click the **Use Floating License** button. To open this dialog manually, select **Help** > **License Manager**.
3. In the **License Server Connection** dialog, select one of the following:
  1. **FlexNet**. Enter the floating license server name and port (provided by your system or license server administrator). Click**OK**. 
[IMAGE alt='' src=''] If you want to use the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet Three-Server Redundancy - Triad License Server' space='']**Three-Server Redundancy** (Triad License Server), follow this format: 
**Server Name:** hostname1,hostname2,hostname3 (where *hostname1*is the master of the triad)**Port:** 1101 (default port embedded in the floating license key file)If you want to use different Cameo vendor daemon ports for different triad servers, use this format: 
**Server Name:** hostname1,port2@hostname2,port3@hostname3 
**Port:** port1
  2. **DSLS**. Select one of the options:
    1. **Organization defined**. Provides access via the licensing servers specified in a file on the client's computer licensing directory. Can be either set by the user or by the server administrators up front. Click **OK**.
    2. **Custom**. Input the server address (must include the port number, which is 4085 by default. e.g., myaddress:4085). Click **OK**.[IMAGE alt='' src=''] If the**Automatically login each time <modeling tool> is started** check box is selected, the **License Server Connection** dialog will not be displayed, and the licenses will be obtained automatically. To reset the licenses or select additional ones, do the following:In the main menu, click **Options** > **Environment**. The**Environment Options** dialog opens.In the **Floating** options group, set the **Auto Login to the License Server** option to *false*.Restart the modeling tool.[IMAGE alt='' src='']
4. In the **Select Edition/Plugin** dialog, select the modeling tool edition, plugins you want to use, and the floating license connection type: online or offline ([CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Basic concepts' space='']). Click **OK**. 
[IMAGE alt='' src=''] Offline license supportDSLS offline (borrowed) licenses are not supported on macOS/Linux. See the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='DSLS installation and licensing' space=''] page.FlexNet license borrowing is not supported on macOS machines running with ARM Java. See the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='FlexNet license server installation and licensing' space=''] page. To obtain a floating license for your plugin, you must install it in your modeling tool first. Once the plugin is installed, you will find it listed under **Plugins** in the **Select Edition/Plugin** window. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Installing modeling tools and plugins' space=''] To check the license information, select **Help** > **About** and click the **Licensing** tab.

##### Finishing offline floating license session

To finish an offline floating license session earlier

1. In the main menu, click Help > Finish Offline License Session . [ATTACHMENT filename='finish offline license session.png']
2. Click Yes.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726181 space=IL2024x version=4 -->
## PAGE 00055: Obtaining License Keys

- page_id: `136726181`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726181/Obtaining+License+Keys
- version_number: 4
- version_date: `2023-11-16T13:11:46.406+01:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

##### Obtaining software license keys

To request your software license keys, please contact your Dassault Systèmes Sales Contact or Distributor with the necessary technical information.

You can download and complete the [license key request form (XLS)](https://www.3ds.com/assets/Terms/SoftwareKeys/License_Key_Request_Form.xls) for that purpose.

In order to request DSLS or FlexNet license keys, you must first identify the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Basic concepts' space=''] of the computer on which the license key will be installed.

##### Steps to request a FlexNet license keySteps to request a FlexNet license key

1. Determine the Host ID :
  1. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Target ID' space='']
  2. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Host ID or Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed' space='']
2. Send this information to your Sales Contact or Distributor
  1. by filling and sending the above-mentioned form
  2. or by sending the Host ID directly

##### StepsToRequestDSLSLicenseKeySteps to request a DSLS license key

1. Determine the Computer ID for the machine of a node-lock based license or the concurrent/shareable (floating) license:
  1. Download and extract the contents of the following ZIP file to the computer on which you will install the DSLS license key: DSLS target ID executable
  2. Run this command to identify the Computer ID: **DSLicTarget.exe –t** For an alternative option to determine the **Computer ID**for the machine of a node-lock based license, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Target ID' space=''] page.
2. Send this information to your Sales Contact or Distributor
  1. by filling and sending the above-mentioned form
  2. or by sending the Computer ID directly

For more information, see:

- Dassault Systèmes License Server and License Keys
- Software License Keys

## PAGE 00056: Plugins licensing

- page_id: `136726232`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726232/Plugins+licensing
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:19.870+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Modeling tools and plugins licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

500460593

500460595

500460591

**On this page**

4

500460594

##### Adding the license key file

1. In the Resource Plugin Manager dialog, click the Manage Licenses button.
2. In the modeling tool License Manager dialog, click the Select License Key Files button. Then in the Select Key File dialog, select the license key file and click Open .
3. In the License Configuration dialog, check the license information and click OK .
4. When you receive the message to restart the modeling tool, click OK .
5. Restart the modeling tool.

##### Obtaining the floating license

- Make sure your floating license server contains the plugin license.
- Make sure the plugins are installed.

1. Start the modeling tool.
2. On the Help menu, click License Manager .
3. In the modeling tool License Manager dialog, click the Use Floating License button.
4. In the **License Server Connection** dialog, select one of the following:
  1. **FlexNet**. Enter the floating license server name and port (provided by your system or license server administrator). Click **OK**.[IMAGE alt='' src=''] Your system or license server administrator provides the server name and port.
  2. **DSLS**. Select one of the options:
    1. **Organization defined**. Provides access via the licensing servers specified in a file on the client's computer licensing directory. Can be either set by the user or by the server administrators up front. Click **OK**.
    2. **Custom**. Input the server address (must include the port number, which is 4085 by default. e.g., myaddress:4085). Click **OK**.[IMAGE alt='' src=''] If the**Automatically login each time <modeling tool> is started** check box is selected, the **License Server Connection** dialog will not be displayed, and the licenses will be obtained automatically. To reset the licenses or select additional ones, do the following:In the main menu, click **Options** > **Environment**. The**Environment Options** dialog opens.In the **Floating** options group, set the **Auto Login to the License Server** option to *false*.Restart the modeling tool.[IMAGE alt='' src='']
5. In the Select Edition/Plugin dialog, select the edition and plugins. Click OK .

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE
