<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726190 space=IL2024x version=2 -->
## PAGE 00058: Reader Mode activation

- page_id: `136726190`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726190/Reader+Mode+activation
- version_number: 2
- version_date: `2023-11-14T16:17:16.669+01:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

The modeling tool Reader Mode is used to read projects. You will be able to open projects, including server projects, view diagrams, print, and copy as images.

The reader mode is available for all the modeling tools.

##### Prerequisites

- You have the modeling tool installed.

For information about how to download the installation files, see [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading Reader installation files' space=''].

##### Start using the Reader Mode for the first time

To start using the Reader Mode for the first time

1. Start the modeling tool for the first time. The License Manager dialog is displayed.
2. In the License Manager dialog, click the Use in Reader Mode button. The License Agreement window opens.
3. In the License Agreement window, click the I Agree button.

If you were working with the modeling tool's licensed version but need to switch to the Reader Mode, follow the steps of the procedure below.

##### Switching to the Reader Mode

To switch to the Reader Mode

1. In the modeling tool's main menu, click Help > License Manager .
2. In the open License Manager dialog, click the Use in Reader Mode button. The License Agreement window opens.
3. In the License Agreement window, click the I Agree button.
4. Restart the modeling tool.

You can always go back from using the Reader Mode to the licensed modeling tool version.

##### Switching back to the licensed version

To switch back to the licensed version

1. In the modeling tool's main menu, click Help > License Manager .
2. In the open License Manager dialog, do one of the following:
  1. Click the Use Floating License button. Restart the modeling tool.
  2. Click the Select License Key File button. Add the license key and restart the modeling tool.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<p style="text-align: left;">The modeling tool Reader Mode is used to read projects. You will be able to open projects, including server projects, view diagrams, print, and copy as images. </p><p style="text-align: left;">The reader mode is available for all the modeling tools.</p><h3 style="text-align: left;">Prerequisites</h3><ul><li style="text-align: left;">You have the modeling tool installed.</li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="info" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="2a580dd0-15de-41ad-a2af-b55ae7c7dbb7"><ac:rich-text-body><p>For information about how to download the installation files, see <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Downloading Reader installation files" /></ac:link>.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><h3 style="text-align: left;">Start using the Reader Mode for the first time</h3><p style="text-align: left;">To start using the Reader Mode for the first time</p><hr /><ol><li style="text-align: left;">Start the modeling tool for the first time. The <strong>License Manager</strong> dialog is displayed.</li><li style="text-align: left;">In the <strong>License Manager</strong> dialog, click the <strong>Use in Reader Mode</strong> button. The License Agreement window opens.</li><li style="text-align: left;">In the License Agreement window, click the <strong>I Agree</strong> button.</li></ol><p>If you were working with the modeling tool's licensed version but need to switch to the Reader Mode, follow the steps of the procedure below.</p><h3>Switching to the Reader Mode</h3><p>To switch to the Reader Mode</p><hr /><ol><li>In the modeling tool's main menu, click <strong>Help </strong>&gt; <strong>License Manager</strong>.</li><li>In the open <strong>License Manager</strong> dialog, click the <strong>Use in Reader Mode</strong> button. The License Agreement window opens.</li><li>In the License Agreement window, click the <strong>I Agree</strong> button.</li><li>Restart the modeling tool.</li></ol><p style="text-align: left;">You can always go back from using the Reader Mode to the licensed modeling tool version. </p><h3 style="text-align: left;">Switching back to the licensed version</h3><p>To switch back to the licensed version</p><hr /><ol><li>In the modeling tool's main menu, click <strong>Help </strong>&gt; <strong>License Manager</strong>.</li><li>In the open <strong>License Manager</strong> dialog, do one of the following:<ol><li>Click the <strong>Use Floating License</strong> button. Restart the modeling tool.</li><li>Click the <strong>Select License Key File </strong>button. Add the license key and restart the modeling tool.</li></ol></li></ol>
````

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726273 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00059: Replacing a license key on the FlexNet license server

- page_id: `136726273`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726273/Replacing+a+license+key+on+the+FlexNet+license+server
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:21.839+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### EXCERPT: To add a new license file to the floating license server by copying it directly to a specific location

INLINE

You must replace the old floating license key with a new one if:

- You upgrade products to the new version that uses the floating license.
- The Ethernet Address ( [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Determine the Host ID or Target ID of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed' space='IL2024x'] ) of the machine on which the FlexNet license server is installed changes.

To replace a license key

1. [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Adding a license to the FlexNet server' space='IL2024x'] (or use the alternative*).
2. Restart the Vendor Daemon - Cameo:
  1. Connect to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface. The default address is*[http://localhost:8090/](http://localhost:8090/)*or use your server name (*http://<server name>:8090*)
  2. Click the Vendor Daemon Configuration tab.
  3. In the Vendor Daemons list, click the desired daemon and start in again.
  4. Save changes.

* You can copy the new license key directly to a specific location in the floating license server installation folder rather than importing the file by using *lmadmin*. Use this method as an alternative if you cannot import the license key.

#### EXPAND: To add a new license file to the floating license server by copying it directly to a specific location

To add a new license file to the floating license server by copying it directly to a specific location

1. Go to the folder the new license file is stored in and copy the file.
2. Go to <floating license server installation directory>\licenses\cameo and paste the file.
3. Connect to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface. Use the default address ([http://localhost:8090](http://localhost:8090/)) or your server name (http://<server name>:8090).
4. Sign in as the administrator.
5. On the left side menu, click Vendor Daemon Configuration .
6. In the appropriate cameo vendor daemon row, click the Administer button.
7. Click the Reread License Files button. If the license file is successfully imported, you will see an appropriate message on the webpage.
8. Check the active licenses (see the following procedure).
9. If the active licenses are not updated, please restart the floating server.

To check active licenses

1. Connect to the FlexNet License Server management Web interface. The default address is http://localhost:8090/ or use your server name ( http://<server name>:8090 ).
2. Open the **Dashboard.**
3. Click Concurrent. All active licenses are listed in a table.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

## PAGE 00061: Seat licensing

- page_id: `136726186`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726186/Seat+licensing
- version_number: 2
- version_date: `2023-10-23T07:18:35.749+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Sales and licenses
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

##### What is Seat Licensing?

Seat License - the same as a Standalone or "machine" license. The Seat License allows using modeling tools on one Machine where it is installed.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

````html
<h3>What is Seat Licensing?</h3><p>Seat License - the same as a Standalone or &quot;machine&quot; license. The Seat License allows using modeling tools on one Machine where it is installed.</p>
````

## PAGE 00064: System requirements for Teamwork Cloud

- page_id: `136726108`

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

[CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='System requirements' space='TWCloud2024x']true

## PAGE 00065: System requirements for versions 19.0 SP3 and 19.0 SP4

- page_id: `136726107`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726107/System+requirements+for+versions+19.0+SP3+and+19.0+SP4
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:14.325+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > System requirements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

##### The system requirements for 19.0 SP3 and 19.0 SP4 versions

##### Modeling Tools*

| Resource | Recommended |
| --- | --- |
| CPU | Intel Core™ i5 or higher |
| RAM | 16GB |
| Disk space | 1GB or more depending on used plugins |
| Display resolution** | Full HD (1920x1080) or higher |
| Operating Systems | Any Java SE 8-compatible operating system (Windows, Windows Server, Linux (RedHat/CentOS 7), Mac OS X). |
| Java Virtual Machine (JVM) version | Java version support |

* MagicDraw, Cameo Systems Modeler, Cameo Enterprise Architecture

** 800x600, 1280x1024 display resolutions are compatible with a laptop or a projector.

#### NOTE: Earlier versions

Earlier versions

Windows XP and earlier versions are not supported. 
Mac OS 10.6 Snow Leopard and earlier versions are not supported.

##### FLEXnet License Server

For system requirements, refer to the [License Administration Guide](https://www.nomagic.com/files/manuals/fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf) section 8 – “Selecting a License Server Machine” and subsection of section 9 – “System Requirements for lmadmin”.

##### Teamwork Server

| Resource | Minimum | Recommended |
| --- | --- | --- |
| CPU | PentiumTM 3, 800 MHz | PentiumTM 4, 1.4 GHz or higher |
| RAM | 512 MB | 2 GB or more |
| Disk space*** | 25 GB*** | 1 TB or more*** |
| Operating Systems | Any Java SE 8-compatible operating system (Windows, Windows Server 2019, Linux (RedHat/CentOS 7), Mac OS X). |  |
| Java Virtual Machine (JVM) version | Java version support |  |

###### For Unix platforms, XWindow server is required for starting Teamwork Server with GUI and Teamwork Server Console.

******* Use the [formula](https://www.nomagic.com/products/teamwork-server#formula) to estimate the storage required for the Teamwork Server disk space.

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726109 space=IL2024x version=6 -->
## PAGE 00066: System requirements for Web Application Platform

- page_id: `136726109`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726109/System+requirements+for+Web+Application+Platform
- version_number: 6
- version_date: `2026-02-12T16:01:13.001+01:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > System requirements
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

Cameo Collaborator for Teamwork Cloud is a web-based product and supports the latest versions of Microsoft Edge, Chrome, Firefox, and Safari.

##### System requirements for small and medium deployments

Small and medium deployments are deployments where 5, 10, 25, or 50 connection licenses are used.

System requirements:

- 32 GB of RAM dedicated exclusively to Web Application Platform services and additional RAM per OS requirements
- 100 GB of free space on the disk, NVMe or SSD
- CPU with 8 cores running at 2.1 GHz
- Windows 2016, Windows 2019, Linux 64-bit RedHat/CentOS 7, or RedHat 8
- OpenJDK 17
- For deployments on Linux, the open file limit must be no less than 20,000 files.

##### System requirements for large enterprise deployments

Large enterprise deployments are deployments where 75, 100, or unlimited connection licenses are used.

System requirements for deployments using 75 or 100 connection licenses:

- 64 GB of RAM dedicated exclusively to Web Application Platform services and additional RAM per OS requirements
- 200 GB of free space on the disk, preferably SSD
- CPU with 16 cores running at 2.1 GHz
- Windows 2016, Windows 2019, Linux 64-bit RedHat/CentOS 7, or RedHat 8
- Java 17
- For deployments on Linux, the open file limit must be no less than 20,000 files.

#### NOTE: Deployments with unlimited licenses

Deployments with unlimited licenses

If you have a deployment with an unlimited license or are in doubt about what hardware to use, contact your account executive for hardware recommendations to accommodate your specific needs.

#### NOTE: Note on Web Application Platform

Note on Web Application Platform

When installing Web Application Platform for production purposes, it is recommended to [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Web Application Platform Installation on a separate machine' space='MCS2024x'].

## PAGE 00067: Troubleshooting

- page_id: `136726279`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726279/Troubleshooting
- version_number: 4
- version_date: `2025-09-24T09:55:46.226+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

#### EXCERPT: A script is intended for CentOS and RedHat

INLINE

###### JRE libraries are missing or not compatible

Error message while installing 32-bit *lmadmin* on 64-bit multi-arch Linux system.

The error message is misleading, the solution to fix it, is to install the 32-bit libraries.

In**Redhat/CentOS/Fedora**:

```text

```

In **recent Ubuntu** use:

```text

```

In**older Ubuntu** use:

```text

```

###### No such file or directory running *lmadmin*

That may mean that you are missing the correct Linux Standard Base (LSB) library.

Also, it may mean that you are using a 64-bit executable in a 32-bit system and vice versa.

Install the Linux Standard Base (LSB) libraries to fix it.

**[libssl.so](http://libssl.so).1.0.0 library required running *lmadmin***

*lmadmin* 11.17.0 comes with [libssl.so](http://libssl.so).* in its installation directory. 
You need to add these libraries in *lmadmin* directory to the LD_LIBRARY_PATH. 
 
e.g. if your *lmadmin* installation is at /opt/FNPLicenseServerManager then adding it to the path would look like this:

```text

```

###### *lmadmin* won't start

If you install *lmadmin* on a Linux-based system when logged on as root, you may encounter various issues. For example:

- When you try to launch the Web server ( http://localhost:port ) on the license server, you encounter an "Unable to connect" error.
- When you attempt to run the license server, you may encounter the following errors:

In Web.log:

- A process listing for lmadmin ('ps aux | grep lmadmin ') returns no results.
- A process listing for cameo ('ps aux|grep cameo') returns results if run right after lmadmin is started but then fails after a few seconds. If you view the cameo.log file in the logs directory (the default location is /opt/FNPLicenseServerManager/logs), you see that the process failed with the following error messages:

Therefore, when you are installing *lmadmin* on a Linux-based system, it is recommended that you avoid installing as root. If you have already installed *lmadmin* when logged on as root and you do not want to reinstall *lmadmin*, change the ownership of all of the files in the installed folder from root to another user

###### 'Can't make directory' error running *lmgrd*

Can't make directory /usr/tmp/.flexlm, errno: 2(No such file or directory).

This means that directory /usr/tmp used by *lmgrd* is missing on your system (usually on Ubuntu systems). This error does not impact license checkout.

The solution to fix it is to create a symbolic link /usr/tmp pointing to /tmp:

```text

```

###### You have no permission to install *lmadmin* in that directory

Make sure the *lmadmin* installer has read/write access.

```text

```

or

```text

```

to give read/write privileges to all files within a folder.

Then run*lmadmin*using sudo:

```text
]]>
```

###### A sample script that performs the automated installation of *lmadmin 11.14 from [nomagic.com](http://nomagic.com)* in case you need it for reference purposes

```text
/dev/null || groupadd -r lmadmin
sudo getent passwd lmadmin >/dev/null || useradd -d /home/lmadmin -g lmadmin -m -r lmadmin
sudo yum install -y ld-linux.so.2
LSB=$(yum provides /lib/ld-lsb.so.3 | grep lsb-core | tail -1 | cut -f 1 -d ' ')
sudo yum install -y $LSB
sudo echo "lmadmin ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL " >> /etc/sudoers
# If Web GUI to Flex licensing is not a must - lmgrd can be used, can be placed in rc.local to startup on boot
# usage - ./lmgrd -c PATH_TO_KEY_FILE -l PATH_TO_LOG_FILE
# RW rights needed to both files
echo "==========================================================="
echo "Getting Linux 32-bit IPv6 version 11.14 from AWS FrontCloud"
echo "==========================================================="
wget http://d1g91r27pzl568.cloudfront.net/Cameo_daemon/FlexNet_11_14/ipv6/linux/lnx_32/cameo
chmod +x cameo
echo "========================================"
echo "Getting Linux 32-bit lmgrd version 11.14"
echo "========================================"
wget https://d1oqhepk9od1tu.cloudfront.net/Flex_License_Server_Utilities/v11.14/linux32/lmgrd
chmod +x lmgrd
echo "======================================"
echo "Making flex log file named FlexLog.log"
echo "======================================"
touch FlexLog.log
chmod 664 FlexLog.log
echo "=========================================="
echo "Getting Linux 32-bit lmadmin version 11.14"
echo "=========================================="
wget https://d1oqhepk9od1tu.cloudfront.net/Flex_License_Server_Utilities/v11.14/linux32/lmadmin-i86_lsb-11_14_0_0.bin
chmod +x lmadmin-i86_lsb-11_14_0_0.bin
echo "========================================="
echo "Executing lmadmin version 11.14 installer"
echo "IMPORTANT: Install into directory /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager"
echo ""
echo " Note:  Accept all defaults for script to work properly!!!"
read -p -"Press any key to continue ...: " -n1 -s
echo "=========================================="
sudo ./lmadmin-i86_lsb-11_14_0_0.bin
sudo mkdir -p /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/licenses/cameo/
sudo cp cameo /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/cameo
sudo mv cameo /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/licenses/cameo/cameo
sudo mv lmgrd /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lmgrd
sudo mv FlexLog.log /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/FlexLog.log
sudo chown -R lmadmin:lmadmin /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/
sudo chmod +x /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lib*
sudo cp /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lib* /usr/lib/
echo "======================"
echo "Opening firewall ports"
echo "======================"
FWZONE=$(sudo firewall-cmd --get-default-zone)
cat <

    lmadmin
    lmadmin
    
    

EOF
sleep 5
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=public --remove-port=8090/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=public --remove-port=1101/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=public --remove-port=27000-27009/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=internal --remove-port=8090/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=internal --remove-port=1101/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=internal --remove-port=27000-27009/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=$FWZONE --add-service=lmadmin --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --reload
IP_ADDRESS=$(ip route get 1 | awk '{print $NF;exit}')
HOSTNAME=$(hostname)
echo "$IP_ADDRESS     $HOSTNAME" >> /etc/hosts 
echo "=========================================="
echo "Creating systemd service - lmadmin"
echo "=========================================="
sudo echo "[Unit]" > /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "Description=Flexnet License Daemon" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "After=network.target network.service" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "[Service]" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "User=lmadmin" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "WorkingDirectory=/opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "ExecStart=/opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lmadmin -allowStopServer yes" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "Restart=always" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "RestartSec=30" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "Type=forking" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "[Install]" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "WantedBy=multi-user.target" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo chown root:root /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo chmod 755 /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo systemctl daemon-reload
sudo systemctl enable lmadmin.service
echo "=========================================="
echo "lmadmin service installation complete"
echo "  usage: systemctl start|stop lmadmin"
echo "=========================================="]]>
```

If you run into any further problems with installation, please try:

- checking the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Frequently Asked Questions' space='FAQ'] for the known problems
- contacting [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Support' space='NMDOC']

If you view the cameo.log file in the logs directory (the default location is /opt/FNPLicenseServerManager/logs), you see that the process failed with the following error messages:</li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="noformat" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="17b95a8e-e95c-41b8-9c73-455fb951b1b0"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[ 07:55:17 (cameo) Report log started (cameo/report.log).
 07:55:27 (cameo) Vendor daemon can't talk to lmgrd (Cannot read data from license server system. (-16,287))
 07:55:27 (cameo) EXITING DUE TO SIGNAL 37 Exit reason 5]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p>Therefore, when you are installing <em>lmadmin</em> on a Linux-based system, it is recommended that you avoid installing as root. If you have already installed <em>lmadmin</em> when logged on as root and you do not want to reinstall <em>lmadmin</em>, change the ownership of all of the files in the installed folder from root to another user</p><h4>'Can't make directory' error running <em>lmgrd</em></h4><p>Can't make directory /usr/tmp/.flexlm, errno: 2(No such file or directory).</p><p><br /></p><p>This means that directory /usr/tmp used by <em>lmgrd</em> is missing on your system (usually on Ubuntu systems). This error does not impact license checkout.</p><p>The solution to fix it is to create a symbolic link /usr/tmp pointing to /tmp:</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="8c970dd5-f7c8-46bf-a998-802a276095f0"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[ln -s /tmp /usr/tmp]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><h4>You have no permission to install <em>lmadmin</em> in that directory</h4><p>Make sure the <em>lmadmin</em> installer has read/write access.</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="dd829450-528a-404d-8a0d-864e72054ce1"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[chmod 755 lmadmin]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><span>or</span></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="2f0d610a-8a84-402a-88c4-3ee143d05f5e"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[chmod -R 755 folder_containing_lmadmin]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><span>to give read/write privileges to all files within a folder.</span></p><p><span> </span></p><p><span>Then run </span><em>lmadmin</em><span> using sudo:</span></p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="9338b1e6-6883-4384-a59b-04a700114ac5"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[sudo ./<lmadmin_installer>]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><h4>A sample script that performs the automated installation of <em>lmadmin 11.14 from <a href="http://nomagic.com">nomagic.com</a></em> in case you need it for reference purposes</h4><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="ab322a06-fc5c-4e12-9d7f-cabbbdfbcff9"><ac:parameter ac:name="title">A script is intended for CentOS and RedHat</ac:parameter><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[#!/bin/bash
echo "==============="
echo "Installing wget"
echo "==============="
sudo yum install -y wget
echo "=================="
echo "Installing lmadmin"
echo "=================="
sudo getent group lmadmin >/dev/null || groupadd -r lmadmin
sudo getent passwd lmadmin >/dev/null || useradd -d /home/lmadmin -g lmadmin -m -r lmadmin
sudo yum install -y ld-linux.so.2
LSB=$(yum provides /lib/ld-lsb.so.3 | grep lsb-core | tail -1 | cut -f 1 -d ' ')
sudo yum install -y $LSB
sudo echo "lmadmin ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL " >> /etc/sudoers
# If Web GUI to Flex licensing is not a must - lmgrd can be used, can be placed in rc.local to startup on boot
# usage - ./lmgrd -c PATH_TO_KEY_FILE -l PATH_TO_LOG_FILE
# RW rights needed to both files
echo "==========================================================="
echo "Getting Linux 32-bit IPv6 version 11.14 from AWS FrontCloud"
echo "==========================================================="
wget http://d1g91r27pzl568.cloudfront.net/Cameo_daemon/FlexNet_11_14/ipv6/linux/lnx_32/cameo
chmod +x cameo
echo "========================================"
echo "Getting Linux 32-bit lmgrd version 11.14"
echo "========================================"
wget https://d1oqhepk9od1tu.cloudfront.net/Flex_License_Server_Utilities/v11.14/linux32/lmgrd
chmod +x lmgrd
echo "======================================"
echo "Making flex log file named FlexLog.log"
echo "======================================"
touch FlexLog.log
chmod 664 FlexLog.log
echo "=========================================="
echo "Getting Linux 32-bit lmadmin version 11.14"
echo "=========================================="
wget https://d1oqhepk9od1tu.cloudfront.net/Flex_License_Server_Utilities/v11.14/linux32/lmadmin-i86_lsb-11_14_0_0.bin
chmod +x lmadmin-i86_lsb-11_14_0_0.bin
echo "========================================="
echo "Executing lmadmin version 11.14 installer"
echo "IMPORTANT: Install into directory /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager"
echo ""
echo " Note:  Accept all defaults for script to work properly!!!"
read -p -"Press any key to continue ...: " -n1 -s
echo "=========================================="
sudo ./lmadmin-i86_lsb-11_14_0_0.bin
sudo mkdir -p /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/licenses/cameo/
sudo cp cameo /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/cameo
sudo mv cameo /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/licenses/cameo/cameo
sudo mv lmgrd /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lmgrd
sudo mv FlexLog.log /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/FlexLog.log
sudo chown -R lmadmin:lmadmin /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/
sudo chmod +x /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lib*
sudo cp /opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lib* /usr/lib/
echo "======================"
echo "Opening firewall ports"
echo "======================"
FWZONE=$(sudo firewall-cmd --get-default-zone)
cat <<EOF | sudo tee /etc/firewalld/services/lmadmin.xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<service version="1.0">
    <short>lmadmin</short>
    <description>lmadmin</description>
    <port port="8090" protocol="tcp"/>
    <port port="1101" protocol="tcp"/>
</service>
EOF
sleep 5
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=public --remove-port=8090/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=public --remove-port=1101/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=public --remove-port=27000-27009/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=internal --remove-port=8090/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=internal --remove-port=1101/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=internal --remove-port=27000-27009/tcp --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --zone=$FWZONE --add-service=lmadmin --permanent
sudo firewall-cmd --reload
IP_ADDRESS=$(ip route get 1 | awk '{print $NF;exit}')
HOSTNAME=$(hostname)
echo "$IP_ADDRESS     $HOSTNAME" >> /etc/hosts 
echo "=========================================="
echo "Creating systemd service - lmadmin"
echo "=========================================="
sudo echo "[Unit]" > /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "Description=Flexnet License Daemon" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "After=network.target network.service" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "[Service]" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "User=lmadmin" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "WorkingDirectory=/opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "ExecStart=/opt/local/FNPLicenseServerManager/lmadmin -allowStopServer yes" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "Restart=always" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "RestartSec=30" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "Type=forking" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "[Install]" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "WantedBy=multi-user.target" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo echo "" >> /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo chown root:root /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo chmod 755 /etc/systemd/system/lmadmin.service
sudo systemctl daemon-reload
sudo systemctl enable lmadmin.service
echo "=========================================="
echo "lmadmin service installation complete"
echo "  usage: systemctl start|stop lmadmin"
echo "=========================================="]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p><span style="color:var(--ds-text,#000000);"> </span></p><p><span style="color:var(--ds-text,#000000);">If you run into any further problems with installation, please try:</span></p><ul><li data-uuid="b4da7678-352b-4f87-b9e6-96f0bc70269b"><span style="color:var(--ds-background-accent-red-bolder,#c9372c);"><span style="color:var(--ds-text,#000000);">checking the</span> <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="FAQ" ri:content-title="Frequently Asked Questions" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[FAQ section]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> <span style="color:var(--ds-text,#000000);">for the known problems</span></span></li><li data-uuid="7cd1cf12-a981-4646-a3e4-2b27ac8b5c29"><span style="color:var(--ds-text,#000000);">contacting <ac:link><ri:page ri:space-key="NMDOC" ri:content-title="Support" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[customer support]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link></span></li></ul></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro>
````

## PAGE 00068: Uninstalling FlexNet license server

- page_id: `136726274`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726274/Uninstalling+FlexNet+license+server
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:21.932+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > FlexNet license server installation and licensing
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

476790241

476790253

476790243

INLINE

To uninstall the FlexNet license server

1. Go to the FlexNet Server Publisher web interface. Use the default address ([http://localhost:8090](http://localhost:8090/)) or your server name ([http://](http://docs.nomagic.com/)<server name>:8090).
2. Stop the server process:
  - Click the **Stop Server** button in the Administration section to stop the license manager and the vendor daemon.
  - End the lmadmin task process in:
    - Task Manager on Windows
    - Activity Monitor on OS X
    - System Monitor on Linux
3. Uninstall the server with an uninstaller specific to your operating system.

906118869

**For more information about uninstalling the FlexNet license server, see:**

- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.19.0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.18.2.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_17_0.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11.16.4.pdf']
- [ATTACHMENT filename='fnp_LicAdmin_11_12_1.pdf']

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726240 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00069: Uninstalling modeling tools and plugins

- page_id: `136726240`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726240/Uninstalling+modeling+tools+and+plugins
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:20.063+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

602068638

602068659

602068637

**On this page**

****

602068649

INLINE

##### **Uninstalling modeling tools**

**Uninstall on Windows**

- In the <modeling tool> installation > UninstallerData folder, double-click the Uninstall <modeling tool> file.

**Uninstall on OS X**

- Right-click the <modeling tool> installation folder and from the shortcut menu, select Move to Trash .

**Uninstall on Unix**

- In the <modeling tool> installation > UninstallerData folder, double-click the Uninstall <modeling tool> file.

##### Removing no-install package

**Windows**

- Delete the <modeling tool> installation folder.

**OS X**

- Right-click the <modeling tool> installation folder, and then, from the shortcut menu, select Move to Trash .

**Unix**

- Delete the <modeling tool> installation folder.

##### Uninstalling plugins

1. Start the modeling tool.
2. In the Help menu, select Resource/Plugin Manager .
3. In the Resource/Plugin Manager dialog, click to select the plugin.
4. Click the Remove button.
5. When you receive the message asking if you want to remove the plugin, click OK .
6. Restart the modeling tool.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

INLINE

- Find out the shared object dependencies in Linux. The result can show what files are missing libraries to run that file.

```text
]]>
```

- File information in Linux

```text
]]>
```

- Launching lmgrd manually via command line. lmgrd , cameo, and license file must be in the same directory:

```text
-l ]]>
```

*license_file_name*- the path to the license file. Can use only the license file name if all files are in the same directory.

*logfile_name* - the path to the log file. Can use only the license file name if all files are in the same directory. Make sure the files have read/write privileges.

- Checking server status:

```text
@]]>
```

*server_port* - the port the server is operating on (Not the cameo daemon port)

*server_host_or_ip_address* - the host/address the server is hosted on

Prior to using the command, locate*lmutil*for a particular OS in the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Downloading installation files' space='']**<*product folder*****>\****Flex_Utilities_User_Guides_Vendor_Daemons\<*FlexNet version*>\Server utilities**folder.Navigate to the file via the command line and then execute the command above.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE

The result can show what files are missing libraries to run that file.</li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="ac1d78fb-9ae7-4688-983d-32bd2cb6c18d"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[ldd <file_name>]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ul><li class="auto-cursor-target">File information in Linux</li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="b7fa88e4-72fa-430f-b969-55b9ef4b0b82"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[file <file_name>]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><ul><li>Launching <em>lmgrd</em> manually via command line. <em>lmgrd</em>, cameo, and license file must be in the same directory:</li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="5069fe11-fa85-42e3-893c-1ee5e467d055"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[ lmgrd -c <license_file_name> -l <logfile_name>]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p><em style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">license_file_name</em><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> - the path to the license file. Can use only the license file name if all files are in the same directory. Make sure the files have read/write privileges.</p><ul><li>Checking server status:</li></ul><ac:structured-macro ac:name="code" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="e7557161-b001-4d4b-90ef-6d6bf077f361"><ac:plain-text-body><![CDATA[ lmutil lmstat -a -c <server_port>@<server_host_or_ip_address>]]></ac:plain-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><em>server_port</em> - the port the server is operating on (Not the cameo daemon port)</p><p><em>server_host_or_ip_address</em> - the host/address the server is hosted on</p><ac:structured-macro ac:name="info" ac:schema-version="1" ac:macro-id="3ca778b5-f69c-493d-a065-bb2280dd0dc6"><ac:rich-text-body><p>Prior to using the command, l<span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">ocate </span><em style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">lmutil</em><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> for a particular OS in the <ac:link><ri:page ri:content-title="Downloading installation files" /><ac:plain-text-link-body><![CDATA[downloaded]]></ac:plain-text-link-body></ac:link> </span><strong style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">&lt;<em>product folder</em></strong><strong>&gt;<span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">\</span></strong><strong style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;">Flex_Utilities_User_Guides_Vendor_Daemons\&lt;<em>FlexNet version</em>&gt;\Server utilities</strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0.0px;"> folder. </span>Navigate to the file via the command line and then execute the command above.</p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p></ac:rich-text-body></ac:structured-macro><p class="auto-cursor-target"><br /></p>
````

<!--NOMAGIC_PAGE id=136726283 space=IL2024x version=1 -->
## PAGE 00072: Using modeling tools bundle

- page_id: `136726283`
- space_key: `IL2024x`
- source_url: https://docs.nomagic.com/spaces/IL2024x/pages/136726283/Using+modeling+tools+bundle
- version_number: 1
- version_date: `2023-09-21T13:03:23.040+02:00`
- ancestors: Installation, Licensing, and System Requirements Documentation > Modeling tools bundle
- labels: []

### NORMALIZED CONTENT

##### Using a modeling tools bundle (instructions for an employee)

To use the modeling tools bundle

1. Save the modeling tools bundle on your computer.
2. Extract the bundle.
3. To start the modeling tool, in the <modeling tool installation folder>/bin folder, double-click the <modeling_tool_name>.exe . The modeling tool is started.
4. It is recommended that users create a shortcut to the modeling tool on their desktop or a location of their choice.
5. Point to the license key file provided by the administrator or connect to the floating license server (modeling tool application > Help main menu > License Manager ). You are ready to use the modeling tool.

- For more information about modeling tools licensing, see the [CONFLUENCE_PAGE title='Modeling tools and plugins licensing' space='IL2024x'] page.
- Because the modeling tools bundle is not installed on an employee computer but only shared on it, there will be no application icon on the desktop or in the main menu to open the modeling tool. You can add these items manually.

### EXACT CONFLUENCE STORAGE SOURCE
